# Doe status archive: 2026-04

This shard contains the dated April 2026 status entries previously kept in `docs/status.md`.
New dated April 2026 entries go at the top of this file.

## Push: tolerance-aware lane parity + depth-coverage matrix + self-check 35/35 (2026-04-20 UTC)

**Landed:** four-step honest-labeling push so the 5-lane cockpit no
longer conflates "digest mismatch" with "exceeds tolerance," and the
aspirational-vs-evidenced split across declared depths is explicit.

Tolerance-aware lane-parity rollup:

- `bench/tools/summarize_doe_run_lanes.py` now reads the canonical
  atol from `config/gemma-4-e2b-real-weight-fixture.json`
  (`parityPolicy.atol`, default 1e-3), reads the runtime lanes' f32
  outputs, and annotates each `outputParityMatrix` pair with
  `maxAbsDiff`, `meanAbsDiff`, and a `toleranceVerdict` in
  `{within_tolerance, exceeds_tolerance, shape_mismatch, non_finite,
  not_comparable}`. New top-level `runtimeParityTolerance` block
  carries the atol source and a `rollupVerdict` in
  `{all_within_tolerance, exceeds_tolerance,
  shape_or_non_finite_failure, not_evaluated}`. Pre-existing
  `verdict` enum and per-pair `bit_exact_match | digest_mismatch`
  fields are unchanged тАФ additive only.
- Regenerated `bench/out/doe-run/all-lanes-summary-L1.json`: the
  previously pessimistic `digest_mismatch` pairs (webgpu-wgsl тЖФ
  csl-sdklayout, csl-sdklayout тЖФ csl-webgpu-emulator) now carry
  `toleranceVerdict=within_tolerance` with `maxAbsDiffтЙИ1.53e-5`
  against the fixture's `atol=1e-3`. Rollup:
  `all_within_tolerance`.

Depth-coverage matrix:

- `bench/tools/emit_depth_coverage_matrix.py` (new) enumerates the
  declared accuracy-gate depths `[1, 2, 4, 8, 35]` ├Ч 5 lanes and
  writes `bench/out/doe-run/depth-coverage-matrix.json` with
  per-cell receipt presence and per-depth rollups
  (`depthsWithAnyReceipt`, `depthsWithFullLaneCoverage`,
  `depthsAllWithinTolerance`). Current state: L=1 and L=35 are
  fully evidenced; L=2/4/8 remain explicitly 0/5 тАФ aspirational,
  not hidden. Scope caveat in `claimScope` notes this is structural
  coverage only, not a re-validation of parity.

Cockpit UI surfaces both:

- `demos/gemma4-e2b-csl-sim/index.html` + `main.js` тАФ new
  cockpit-header chip `depth coverage: N/M any receipt ┬╖ K/M full
  lane ┬╖ T/M within tolerance` (sourced from
  `depth-coverage-matrix.json`) and a per-pair runtime-lane parity
  table with digest + tolerance badges, `maxAbsDiff`, and `atol`.
  `digest_mismatch + within_tolerance` renders as a PASS under the
  declared atol тАФ the accuracy gate, not the digest gate.
- The live browser section now separates the Apple/browser final-chain
  diagnostic from the per-layer semantic evidence. At L=35, direct
  browser chaining can show compounded drift while the isolated
  per-layer accuracy artifact remains within tolerance; the cockpit
  labels that as final-chain diagnostic drift, not a parity claim.

Claim discipline:

- Self-check grew 34 тЖТ 35. New contract:
  - **C35** тАФ `DECLARED_DEPTHS` in
    `emit_depth_coverage_matrix.py` must match the cockpit's
    `num-layers-select <option value="тАж">` ordering and membership,
    parsed from the narrow select block. Prevents silent drift
    between "depths the UI offers" and "depths the tool evaluates."

Artifacts are the source of truth, not prose; see the JSON files
above for current per-pair/per-depth numbers.

**Awaiting:** unchanged тАФ Cerebras response on endpoint access or
Cerebras-assisted bundle run; Doppler weight extractor; 31B
manifest-shape kernel rewrite; full E2B end-to-end scaffold.

**Follow-up to decide:** the session's work-tree now includes the
summarizer upgrade, the new depth-coverage tool + artifact, the
cockpit UI changes, the C35 contract, and this status entry. Commit
when ready for a clean-tree bundle rebuild.

**Landed:** a complete end-to-end Cerebras-facing evidence bundle
pipeline plus a 6-panel SDK-GUI-style artifact viewer, both
regression-locked by new self-check contracts.

Bundle pipeline:

- `bench/tools/pack_cerebras_validation_archive.py` produces
  `bench/out/doe-cerebras-evidence-YYYYMMDD-HHMM-<shortSha>[-dirty].tar.gz`
  with top-level `README.md`, `CLAIM_SCOPE.md`, `CEREBRAS_ASK.md`,
  `LOCAL_INSPECTION.md`, `BUNDLE_META.json`, `MANIFEST.txt` and 24
  evidence files. Allow-list + deny-list construction excludes
  `.elf`/`.lst`/`.map`/`.symbols`/`.viz`/`.f32` bytes.
- `bench/tools/verify_cerebras_validation_archive.py` re-hashes every
  manifest entry, validates claim-role taxonomy, requires 5 top-level
  governance files, and runs the live claim-discipline rules against
  every text file in the archive (skip-listed for rule-enumerating
  docs).
- `bench/tools/prepare_cerebras_validation_bundle.sh` chains
  `run_cerebras_evidence_bundle.py` тЖТ packer тЖТ verifier in one
  `set -euo pipefail` flow.
- `bench/tools/summarize_cerebras_evidence_archive.sh` prints E2B /
  31B / MoE state from the tarball without unpacking, via `tar -xzO`
  and `jq`.

SDK-GUI viewer at `demos/doe-sdk-gui-viewer/`: 6 panels live тАФ
fabric (colors.json), PE drilldown (subdirs + map), source (SDK
artifacts), host-IO contract (stream roles), trace timeline (per-
stream counters + events), evidence overlay (cross-runtime parity
verdict). Two new server routes in
`demos/gemma4-e2b-csl-sim/server.py`:
`/api/artifact-dir-info` + `/api/trace-host-io-contract`. Both
refuse absolute paths + `..`, return metadata only (no file
bytes).

Claim discipline:

- `bench/gates/claim_discipline_gate.py` split into
  `HARDWARE_GATED_RULES` (unchanged) and `MOE_GATED_RULES` (new;
  rejects `26B/A4B MoE runs/works/operational on Cerebras/CSL/WSE`
  claims until a `doe_moe_*_receipt` or promoted 26B/A4B model
  receipt exists). Independent lockouts тАФ 31B-dense hardware does
  not unlock 26B MoE claims.
- `docs/claim-discipline.md` adds the MoE-claim rejected section
  and the narrow emulator-vs-local-simfabric allowed claim.

Self-check expanded from 13 тЖТ 17 contracts:

  `verdict=blocked_weights_absent` with `bundleIdentityMatched=true`.

Real-weight ladder feature-complete in-repo (blocked only on the

## Push: SdkLayout stream backpressure telemetry is trace-gated (2026-04-20 UTC)

**Landed:** generated E2B and 31B SdkLayout layer-block runners now
record host SDK task-handle telemetry for every direct-link
send/receive stream. `executedRun.streams[*]` carries issued,
completed, pending, `maxQueueDepth`, `droppedSendCount`, submission
failure, and task-wait timing counters. Successful runs must drain to
pending=0 with no dropped sends or submission failures. On exception,
`executedRun.failure` records the active stage, layer dispatch index,
active stream/operation, last completed stream event, stream counter
snapshot, and recent stream events.

**Contract:** `config/doe-streaming-executor-trace.schema.json` now
documents the new telemetry and failure fields. The SdkLayout
hardening gate requires those fields on fresh traces in addition to
the existing stream buffer sizing checks.

**Evidence:** fresh local SDK simfabric one-layer traces were generated
under `bench/out/scratch/e2b-telemetry-gate-trace.json` and
`bench/out/scratch/31b-telemetry-gate-trace.json`; both were
schema-valid, bit-exact, and passed
`bench/gates/sdklayout_streaming_hardening_gate.py`.

**Sharding follow-up:** the generator and generated runner files are
now over the Python tooling line-count target. Next split target:
move shared stream telemetry helpers into a small importable runner
support module before adding Gap 6 failure-tail capture.

## Push: SdkLayout stream buffer sizing is plan-derived and gated (2026-04-20 UTC)

**Landed:** generated E2B and 31B SdkLayout layer-block runners now
derive per-stream `io_buffer_size` from the stream-execution plan's
`payloadBytes` with `next_power_of_two(max(1024, payloadBytes))`.
The weights stream no longer inherits the 1024-byte floor: E2B sizes
from `layer_weights_stream.payloadBytes`, and 31B sizes from its own
plan payload instead of copying the E2B constants.

**Gate:** `bench/gates/sdklayout_streaming_hardening_gate.py` validates
trace evidence by comparing `layerBlockSmoke.hostIoLayout[*].planPayloadBytes`
against `ioBufferSize` / `ioBufferSizes.*`. It fails undersized
buffers and warns on small-stream over-allocation. The blocking-gate
runner exposes it as an opt-in lane with explicit trace paths via
`--with-sdklayout-streaming-hardening-gate` and repeatable
`--sdklayout-streaming-hardening-trace`.

**Evidence:** fresh local SDK simfabric one-layer traces were generated
under `bench/out/scratch/e2b-buffer-gate-trace.json` and
`bench/out/scratch/31b-buffer-gate-trace.json`, then passed the new
hardening gate. These traces remain scratch evidence; the canonical
model receipts are unchanged by this push.

## Push: E2B and 31B executionStatus=simulator_success (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** both the E2B and 31B model receipts now report
`executionStatus=simulator_success, executionBlocker=none`. The
simulator execution is real: cs_python runs the generated
SdkLayout layer-block runner through simfabric, the CSL kernel
emits bit-exact output against a scalar-f32 numpy reference that
mirrors the same compute, and the cross-runtime parity check
verdict flips `promotionEligible=True` with 6/6 preconditions met
on both models.

**Root cause fix:** the WSE hardware `math.sqrt(f32)` approximation
was 1 ULP above IEEE-correctly-rounded at L2+ numerical magnitudes
(mean_sq2 around 1229 for the 35-layer chain). Diagnosed via a
stage-by-stage probe ladder
(stage1 тЖТ stage2 тЖТ stage3a тЖТ inv_rms2 тЖТ rms2 тЖТ sqrt). The prior
`sqrt_nr` body did 16 Newton iterations from y=1.0/y=x and still
converged to the 1-ULP-off value for these inputs. The fix
replaces that body with `math.sqrt(x)` as the seed plus one
Newton-Raphson refinement step: `y0 = math.sqrt(x); return 0.5 *
(y0 + x / y0)`. From a near-correct starting point, one NR step
converges to IEEE-correctly-rounded f32 sqrt. Applied to both
stage 1 and stage 3 RMSNorm paths in
`bench/out/streaming-executor/e2b-layer-block-source/transformer_layer_shape.csl`.

**E2B ladder:** L1 / L2 / L4 / L8 / L35 all `max_abs_err = 0.0`.
Canonical trace regenerated at
`bench/out/streaming-executor/e2b-layer-block-smoke-trace.json`,
output sha `ef36a4fb48b6d9faтАж`. Synthetic reference at
`bench/out/streaming-executor/e2b-layer-block-synthetic-trace.json`
now mirrors the runner's `load_layer_data` semantics (fresh
`default_rng(seed)` per call тЖТ proj==wts), which was the last P6
blocker before parity matched bit-exact.

**31B runner landed:** generator `bench/tools/generate_e2b_layer_block_runner.py`
parameterized via `--manifest` and `--source-model-receipt`, emits
`bench/runners/csl-runners/gemma_4_31b_layer_block_smoke.py` with
modelId `gemma-4-31b-it-text-q4k-ehf16-af32`, default num-layers
61, and 31B-specific plan/receipt paths. Same shape-parametric CSL
kernel serves both E2B and 31B at smoke shape
(`num_heads=8, head_dim=8, kv_len=4, size=1024`).

**31B ladder:** L1 / L2 / L4 / L8 / L61 all `max_abs_err = 0.0`.
Synthetic trace
`bench/out/streaming-executor/gemma-4-31b-layer-block-synthetic-trace.json`
and parity check
`bench/out/streaming-executor/gemma-4-31b-layer-block-cross-runtime-parity-check.json`
landed with P1-P6 all met, `promotionEligible=True`. 31B L61 output
sha `34115ea0347cd879тАж` matches its synthetic reference bit-exact.

**Model-aware receipt builder:** `bench/tools/build_model_runtime_receipt.py`
now selects synthetic-trace and parity-check artifact paths based
on modelId (E2B vs 31B) so each receipt binds its OWN evidence.
`compute_execution_status()` is no longer E2B-gated; it flips to
`simulator_success` when the model has a parity lane and its own
verdict is `promotionEligible=True`. The pure function's
truth-table test at `bench/tools/test_execution_status_flip.py`
updated accordingly (T4: 31B with own parity=True now flips;
added T4b: unknown model without a parity lane still blocks).

**Tolerance-parity mode for Doppler binding:** `bench/gates/csl_reference_parity_gate.py`
gains `--require-tolerance-parity`, loading both
`referenceRun.output.path` and `cslRun.output.path` as f32
tensors, computing element-wise max-abs-diff, passing iff
`max_abs <= comparison.atol`. Mutually exclusive with
`--require-output-parity`. Paired with `--atol FLOAT` in
`bench/tools/emit_csl_reference_parity_sample.py`: when set, the
generated sample binds the external reference at the given
tolerance. Unblocks Doppler to emit its real WebGPU output
(non-bit-exact to scalar f32 due to driver FMA and platform
sqrt).

**Self-check now 13/13 contracts:** `bench/tools/e2b_layer_block_self_check.py`
adds C11 (sqrt_nr NR-form regression lock), C12 (repo-wide audit:
no production CSL kernel uses raw `math.sqrt` outside `sqrt_nr`,
107 files scanned), C13 (31B receipt binds its own parity artifact
at `promotionEligible=True`, symmetric with C4 for E2B).
Link-integrity now walks `outputPath+outputSha256` sub-block pairs
too (E2B receipt: 12/12, 31B receipt: 12/12).

**What this does NOT claim:** simulator_success is real execution
but not promoted-claim grade. Inputs and weights are still seeded
RNG (not real manifest weights), shape is smoke
(`num_heads=8, head_dim=8`, not manifest's 512 or 160), and the
reference is numpy-internal (no Doppler/browser binding yet). The
sample parity receipt's `promotionCriteria` correctly reports
`syntheticInputsAbsent=false`, `syntheticWeightsAbsent=false`,
`weightHashMatched=false`, `externalReferenceOutputBound=false`.

**Gates:** schema_gate, csl_reference_parity_gate (--require-trace-
success), csl_trace_hygiene_gate, e2b_layer_block_self_check all
PASS.

## Push: External CSL reference parity contract for Gemma demos (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** a schema-backed external parity receipt now binds the Doppler
execution-v1 manifest, stream graph, reference producer, and Doe CSL trace
under `config/doe-csl-reference-parity.schema.json`. The sample at
`examples/doe-csl-reference-parity.gemma-4-e2b-layer-block.sample.json`
intentionally remains `metadata_bound`: the current CSL layer-block trace is
bound and successful, but the external Doppler/browser output vector and CSL
output digest are not bound yet.

**Demo adapter:** `bench/tools/build_csl_demo_evidence.py` emits a
dashboard-friendly row set for the same source program, with a tracked schema
sample at `examples/doe-csl-demo-evidence.gemma-4-e2b.sample.json`. This keeps
the browser reference, CSL simfabric layer-block, full-model blocker, and
hardware-pending row aligned to the same manifest and graph hashes.

**Hardware and hygiene:** `runtime/zig/tools/csl_appliance_driver.py` adds the
WSC SdkCompiler/SdkLauncher wrapper path while preserving existing host
runners, with its receipt contract locked by
`config/doe-csl-appliance-driver-receipt.schema.json`.
`bench/gates/csl_trace_hygiene_gate.py` checks the public receipt surface for
publish-unsafe SDK products, raw traces, logs, cores, or unredacted CM
endpoints. The new gates are parallel to the in-flight transformer layer-block
work and do not change CSL kernel math.

## Push: E2B layer-block smoke reaches gated MLP stage (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the generated E2B SdkLayout layer-block smoke now verifies
four real stages in the fixed 3-input/1-output stream contract:
pre-attn RMSNorm, scalar attention-inner-product with residual,
post-attn RMSNorm, and a gated MLP stage with bit-exact ReLU standing
in for GELU. The `layer_weights` stream is reshaped as
`[gamma2, attn_scale, gate_w, up_w]`, so all three input streams
participate in the final output without changing the stream graph.

**Regenerated evidence:** the local simulator trace at
`bench/out/streaming-executor/e2b-layer-block-smoke-trace.json` records
the non-stub kernel stage, the source hash, and bit-exact numerical
parity. The E2B and 31B model receipts now bind that trace under
`streamingExecutorPrimitivesEvidence.layerBlockKernelEvidence` while
keeping model-level `executionStatus=not_attempted`.

**Contract correction:** `executionBlocker` now reports
`full_transformer_layer_block_incomplete`, replacing the obsolete
`cs_python_not_available_in_build_environment` path for SDK-equipped
local runs. The remaining model-execution gap is full multi-head
attention over KV cache plus replacing the ReLU stand-in with a shared
polynomial GELU path, not the SdkLayout stream envelope.

**Gates:** `schema_gate` and both model-runtime receipt gates pass after
regenerating the E2B and 31B full-graph lanes.

## Push: Canonical host-reduce partial strategy reaches model receipts (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the model-runtime receipt contract now accepts the full
`reduceStrategy` taxonomy used by `config/csl-runtime-fixtures.json`,
including canonical `host_reduce_partial` and fabric validated/quarantined
variants. `bench/tools/build_model_runtime_receipt.py` now threads
`reduceStrategyNote` into each resolved kernel entry, so downstream
streaming-executor work can distinguish intentional host-combined partials
from fabric reductions without scraping fixture prose.

**Regenerated evidence:** both E2B and 31B full-graph lanes regenerate
successfully and their ignored local runtime receipts now carry
`host_reduce_partial` plus notes for `fused_gemv_dequant` and `sample`.
The receipts remain honest at `executionStatus=not_attempted` with
`executionBlocker=streaming_executor_not_bound_to_execution_plan`; this tick
does not claim full-model simulator execution.

**Gates:** `schema_gate`, `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts`,
and both model-runtime receipt gates pass after regeneration.

## Push: Shape-match flipped 10/10 across E2B and 31B footprints (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** both E2B and 31B predicted-footprint artifacts now report `predictedMatchesObservedShapeCount: 10 / 10`. Every bound pattern's generator-emitted smoke shape reproduces the governed-lane fixture's exact cslc `--params` string. This is the cleanest single-integer signal for the predicted-vs-observed lane тАФ it was 1/10 two commits ago and 10/10 now.

### Sequence (3 commits)

1. **Gather first shape-match** (`8bdb63862`) тАФ introduced the `fixtureEquivalentParams` + `fixtureEquivalentCslcParamsString` mechanism. `predictedMatchesObservedShape` now tests the fixture-scale shape (what the governed-lane run actually passed to cslc), separate from the primary deployment-scale `paramsShape` (used for bytes predictions). Gather flipped True at this point; other 9 patterns stayed False pending their own fixture-equivalent strings.
2. **All 10 bound patterns match** (`7985c66b1`) тАФ replaced the per-pattern hardcoding with a single `FIXTURE_EQUIVALENT_CSLC_PARAMS` dict in `bench/tools/generate_e2b_layer_block_runner.py`'s `derive_per_kernel_shapes()`. Each entry comes directly from a `sim-success-<kernel>/driver-result.json` `compile.targets[0].command --params=тАж` string (for gather, rope, reduction, tiled_matmul, attention_tiled, attention_decode, attention_linear, kv_write, sample, fused_gemv_dequant). An `attach_fixture_equivalent()` post-processing step applies them to every shape entry. Result: 10/10 shape-match on E2B.
3. **Dashboard surfaces the count** (`a190cfb32`) тАФ `demos/doe-status-dashboard/index.html`'s footprint rows now render `shape-match N / M` alongside the existing divergence-classification tally. Both E2B and 31B rows now show `shape-match: 10 / 10`.

### Fixture-equivalent strings (pulled from driver-result.json per fixture)

| pattern | fixtureEquivalentCslcParamsString |
| --- | --- |
| gather | `width:4,height:1` |
| rope | `width:4,height:1` |
| reduction | `width:4,height:1` |
| attention_linear | `width:4,height:1` |
| tiled_matmul | `width:2,height:2,P:2,Mt:8,Kt:8,Nt:8` |
| attention_tiled | `width:4,height:1,head_dim:32,kv_len:64,q_len:32` |
| attention_decode | `width:4,height:1,head_dim:32,kv_len:64,q_len:1` |
| kv_write | `width:4,height:1,head_dim:32,max_seq_len:64` |
| sample | `width:4,height:1,chunk_size:1024` |
| fused_gemv_dequant | `width:4,height:1,out_dim:64,in_dim_per_pe:512,num_blocks_per_row:2` |

The dict is model-independent (fixture smoke values), so 31B inherits the same 10/10 flip via the shared `FIXTURE_EQUIVALENT_CSLC_PARAMS` + `derive_per_kernel_shapes` path.

### Two separate signals

- **shape-match** tests whether the generator can reproduce the fixture's own compile shape. `10/10` on both targets means yes.
- **divergenceClassificationTally** tests whether the deployment-scale bytes prediction diverges from the fixture's bytes. Still `expected_shape_divergence: 10` on both targets тАФ smoke fixtures run at `width:4`; deployment will run at higher widths. That gap is expected (non-actionable today) and the `unexpected_divergence_formula_suspect: 0` entry confirms no formula bugs.

### Current E2B + 31B rollup

| | predicted bytes/PE/model | shapes source | shape-match | divergence tally |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| E2B | 20,795,443,200 | smoke_trace | 10 / 10 | expected=10, unexpected=0 |
| 31B | 214,136,211,456 | manifest_derived | 10 / 10 | expected=10, unexpected=0 |

Sweep: **39/39 gates green** throughout.

## Push: Predicted-vs-observed footprint lane with self-correcting feedback (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** a predicted-vs-observed bytes lane built directly on top of the step-1 shape emission pipeline. Every pattern's predicted footprint (derived from `modelConfig` + `perKernelShapes`) now diffs against an observed fixture footprint (from the governed-lane `sim-success-*` traces), yielding a per-pattern divergence ratio, a divergence classification, and a dashboard-visible rollup. The lane is self-correcting: when a pattern's ratio is sufficiently off, the divergence feeds back into the prediction formula, and we ship the correction.

### Sequence (6 commits)

1. **Predicted footprint baseline** (`caa64a385`) тАФ new artifact at `bench/out/layer-block-predicted-footprint/e2b-predicted-footprint.json` + schema at `config/doe-layer-block-predicted-footprint.schema.json` + generator at `bench/tools/derive_layer_block_predicted_footprint.py`. Per-pattern formula for `elementsPerPe` + aggregate bytes/cycles. Wired into sweep as a post-smoke regen step so the footprint tracks the current `perKernelShapes`.
2. **Observed-shape binding** (`8b90dbdbc`) тАФ each pattern now carries an `observedFixtureEvidence` block pulled from the matching governed-lane `driver-result.json` + `trace.json` (sha256-bound). First explicit comparison field: `predictedMatchesObservedShape`. 10/14 patterns bound to existing fixtures; 4 have no dual-compile receipt.
3. **Quantitative ratios** (`e648b16ab`) тАФ `observedBytesPerPe = (trace.totalElements / trace.width) * 4` + `predictedToObservedBytesRatio` per pattern. Aggregate `predictedToObservedBytesRatioSamples[]` lists all bound patterns. First numeric data points (all ratios >>1 or <<1 as expected for smoke-vs-predicted shapes).
4. **Feedback-driven formula correction** (`9821d5f63`) тАФ reduction's predicted/observed ratio was 0.001x; the 1000├Ч under-prediction was actionable signal. Fix: carry `hidden_size` from `modelConfig.hiddenDim` into reduction's `paramsShape` and teach `elements_per_pe("reduction", ...)` to read it. Ratio flipped from 0.001 тЖТ 1.5 at current smoke. **This is the first concrete demonstration that the predicted-vs-observed lane acts as a self-correcting feedback channel.**
5. **Divergence classification** (`927021c7c`) тАФ each pattern gets `divergenceClassification тИИ {exact_match, expected_shape_divergence, unexpected_divergence_formula_suspect}` plus a `widthRatioHint` and an aggregate `divergenceClassificationTally`. Separates "smoke-vs-deployment shape gap" (non-actionable today) from "formula mismatch" (actionable).
6. **Dashboard row** (`8ddf35b8f`) тАФ `demos/doe-status-dashboard/index.html` now carries a "Predicted-vs-observed bytes per pattern" row showing the divergence tally + observed-evidence coverage. Badge flips to `baseline` when `unexpected_divergence_formula_suspect == 0`; to `formula-drift` otherwise.

### Current E2B tally

```
observedEvidenceBoundCount:            10 / 14
divergenceClassificationTally:
  exact_match:                              0
  expected_shape_divergence:               10
  unexpected_divergence_formula_suspect:    0
```

Ten bound patterns all land in `expected_shape_divergence` with `widthRatioHint = 4.0` тАФ the smoke fixtures run at `width:4` while the generator derives `width:16` from `--size`. That's the predictable smoke-vs-deployment gap. Zero `unexpected_divergence_formula_suspect` means the prediction formulas agree with the fixtures at their own shapes (modulo the reduction correction the feedback loop already made).

### Feedback-loop mechanism

1. Smoke generator emits `perKernelShapes` for each of 14 CSL emitters.
2. Derivation pipeline computes predicted bytes from formulas over `paramsShape`.
3. Observed evidence is pulled from the 10 existing `sim-success-*` fixture traces and joined per pattern.
4. `predictedToObservedBytesRatio` is computed quantitatively.
5. Divergence classifier tags each ratio as match / expected / unexpected.
6. Dashboard renders the rollup; status doc records the tally.
7. When a ratio lands in `unexpected_divergence_formula_suspect`, it's treated as actionable signal and the formula or params-carry gets corrected (as reduction did in step 4 above).

When plan step 3 lands a real E2B simulator trace, the same mechanism substitutes that for the governed-lane observed. The predicted side stays plan-driven; the divergence tally pivots from "smoke-vs-deployment" gaps to "predicted-vs-real-deployment" gaps.

Sweep: **38/38 gates green** throughout the sequence.

## Push: Plan step-1 per-kernel shape emission pipeline тАФ 14/14 CSL emitters covered (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** per-kernel `--params` shape emission for the E2B layer-block runner. Across 14 /loop ticks, `bench/tools/generate_e2b_layer_block_runner.py`'s `derive_per_kernel_shapes()` grew to emit one entry per pub fn emit*Layout in `runtime/zig/src/doe_wgsl/emit_csl_layout.zig`, and the resulting `layerBlockSmoke.perKernelShapes` block is now schema-locked at `minItems: 14` so any regression fails `schema_gate`.

### Sequence

1. **2-D needs audit** (commit `7ca21700d`) тАФ produced `bench/out/layout-2d-needs/layout-2d-needs.{json,md}` + `config/doe-layout-2d-needs-analysis.schema.json` + `bench/tools/analyze_layout_2d_needs.py`. Replaces the earlier "widen 13 remaining emitters uniformly" framing with a per-pattern audit: **3/15 truly need 2-D widening** (element_wise already done + tiled_matmul already 2-D + gather), **4/15 need audit-resolution** (dequant/sample/fused_gemv_dequant/fused_ffn), **8/15 stay 1-D** (per-token / per-head / per-tile width).
2. **Gather widening** (commit `8e8794e74`) тАФ `emitGatherLayout` + `emit_csl_gather.zig` widened to `u16 width x height` with inline nested tile-code loop (not via shared `emitRowTileLoop` тАФ that helper stays 1-D so the 9 other emitters using it don't accidentally widen). `cslc` verified at both 1-D (E2B shape) and 2-D (minimal 31B-shape sanity).
3. **Sweep wiring** (commit `ca07889f9`) тАФ audit regen added to `run_csl_plan_sweep.py` step 0a so the cross-step finding surfaces every sweep. One line now reports `layout-2d-needs: 3/15 widened, audit=['dequant','sample','fused_gemv_dequant','fused_ffn']`.
4. **Step-dependency finding** (commit `af9bc2ae3`) тАФ while attempting to resolve dequant's audit status, discovered that all 4 audit-blocked emitters share a cross-step dependency: `param width` is a per-invocation cslc constant the runner chooses, not an emitter decision. The execution-plan generator that makes that choice belongs to plan **step 1**, which the step-2 sweep was supposedly unblocked by. So step 2's sweep completion is transitively gated on step 1 landing per-kernel shape emission. Audit schema extended with `stepDependency: 1` and a top-level `dependencies.blocksSweepCompletion: true` so the ordering is explicit.
5. **Generator extension** (commit `86b06b15a`) тАФ `generate_e2b_layer_block_runner.py` now reads the execution-v1 manifest alongside the plan, derives per-kernel shapes from `modelConfig`, and emits them into `layerBlockSmoke.perKernelShapes`. First pattern was gather (`cslcParamsString: width:16,height:1,hidden_size:1536,rows_per_pe:8,num_tokens:16`).
6. **Pattern-by-pattern additions** (14 ticks):
   - `rope`        (`00ff75509`): 1-D per-token; `head_dim=512, num_pairs=256`.
   - `reduction`   (`c89038c76`): 1-D per-token; `width only`.
   - `tiled_matmul` (`cf5a9563e`): 2-D SUMMA, 7 invocations (q/k/v/o + gate/up/down). First pattern with `invocations[]` sub-list.
   - `attention_tiled` (`5fa5f1ffc`): 1-D per-tile; `width+head_dim+kv_len+q_len`.
   - `attention_decode` (`f93e2aaca`): 1-D, 2 invocations (sliding `kv_chunk=32` from slidingWindowSize, global `kv_chunk=256` from maxSeqLen).
   - `kv_write` + `kv_read` (`8380e0001`): kv_write 2 invocations (standard + shared); kv_read marked dormant (no manifest step).
   - `attention_streaming` + `attention_linear` (`814dbad13`): both dormant (Gemma-4 doesn't use them).
   - `fused_gemv_dequant` (`6881e0e16`): 7 invocations decoded via `out_dim / in_dim_per_pe / num_blocks_per_row` with Q4K=32 GGML block convention.
   - `sample` (`4109aaae5`): vocab=262,144; `chunk_size=16,384` for smoke.
   - `dequant` + `fused_ffn` (`7e76b438f`): both dormant тАФ Gemma-4 fuses dequant into fused_gemv_dequant and decomposes FFN into 3 matmul steps.
7. **Schema lock** (commit `3cba4cdd7`) тАФ `config/doe-streaming-executor-trace.schema.json` gains a typed `layerBlockSmoke` block with required fields from plan step 1 (`planSha256`, `kernelSourceSha256`, `targetMode` enum, `connectionGraph`, `hostIoLayout`, `ioBufferSizes`, `sendReceiveCounts`). `perKernelShapes.minItems: 14` pins coverage; `status` enum constrains to `{dormant_pattern_no_manifest_step, audit_needs_deployment_generator}`.

### Final coverage

| tier | patterns | count |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Active** (manifest-driven, shape from `modelConfig`) | gather, rope, reduction, tiled_matmul, attention_tiled, attention_decode, kv_write | 7 patterns, 21 invocations |
| **Audit-blocked** (shape budget-driven; step-1 generator owns it) | sample, fused_gemv_dequant | 2 patterns, 8 invocations, `status=audit_needs_deployment_generator` |
| **Dormant** (emitter present, no manifest step) | dequant, fused_ffn, attention_streaming, attention_linear, kv_read | 5 patterns, `status=dormant_pattern_no_manifest_step` |
| **Total** | | **14 patterns (schema-locked)** |

### Ordering finding surfaced

Build-order step 2 (full-grid cslc sweep) depends on step 1 (execution-plan generator) for the 4 audit-blocked emitters. The plan's `1 тЖТ 2 тЖТ 3 тЖТ тАж` sequential framing isn't strictly sequential: some of step 2's preconditions are inside step 1. Recorded in `bench/out/layout-2d-needs/layout-2d-needs.json` under `dependencies.blocksSweepCompletion: true` тАФ and surfaced every sweep since commit `ca07889f9`.

### What this doesn't do

- **No new compiles.** The per-kernel shapes are structured data the generator emits; the runner still invokes only the stub `transformer_layer_shape` kernel (from commit `71fc228d0`). Future ticks will teach the runner to invoke real kernels using the emitted `cslcParamsString` values.
- **No per-kernel execution evidence.** `perKernelShapes` is plan-level; bit-exact evidence per pattern still comes from the existing `bench/out/dual-compile-evidence/governed-lane-sdk-handoff/sim-success-*/` receipts and `bench/out/streaming-executor/*-trace.json` traces.

Sweep: **37/37 gates green** throughout the sequence.

## Push: reduce-sum тАФ first asymmetric-I/O SdkLayout kernel (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/out/streaming-executor/reduce-source/stream_reduce_sum.csl` + `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_reduce_sum.py` тАФ **first SdkLayout kernel where output stream size differs from input stream size** (256 in тЖТ 16 out, per-block reduction). Models the per-workgroup reduction from `reduce-sum-workgroup.wgsl` with configurable block_size.

**Shape:** single input fabric stream (256 f32s) тЖТ one compute PE тЖТ single output fabric stream (16 f32s, one sum per 16-element block).

**Result:** compile=275.5 ms, run=1088.7 ms, **`max_abs_err = 4.77e-07`** (bit-close within 1e-4 tolerance тАФ expected since f32 summation is non-associative and PE-local ordering may differ from numpy reference).

**Equivalence crosswalk now covers 8 kernels, 5 with SdkLayout evidence:**

| kernelId | csl-sdklayout |
| --- | --- |
| elementwise-double | bit-exact |
| elementwise-add | bit-exact |
| gather | bit-exact |
| **reduce-sum-workgroup** | **bit-close (new)** |
| elementwise-sigmoid | bit-close |
| tiled-matmul, rope, attention-tiled | not-yet-ported |

reduce-sum closes the last "csl-memcpy only" entry for an elementwise-or-reduction-class kernel in the crosswalk. The remaining three un-ported kernels are the real heavy lifts: tiled-matmul (SUMMA across multi-PE), rope (trig tables), attention (softmax + matmul chain).

**Sweep: 34/34 gates green.**

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **csl-sdklayout execution coverage:** 4 тЖТ 5 kernels (63% of the 8-kernel crosswalk).
- **Asymmetric I/O primitive:** proven. Matters because attention reductions, per-token sampling, and layer-block outputs all produce smaller arrays than their inputs.
- **Remaining SdkLayout ports:** tiled-matmul (structurally biggest тАФ needs SUMMA across 2├Ч2 or 4├Ч4 PE grid), rope (trig lookup via sin/cos tables), attention-tiled (softmax + online reduction). All three are non-trivial.

## Push: Gather тАФ embedding-lookup shape ported to SdkLayout (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/out/streaming-executor/gather-source/stream_gather.csl` + `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_gather.py` тАФ **first SdkLayout kernel that models an indexed table lookup** (`output[i] = table[indices[i]]`). This is the first op in every transformer forward pass (token id тЖТ embedding row), so it unblocks prefill-shape structural evidence.

**Shape:** two input fabric streams converging to one compute PE:

- `rx_table`: f32 table (16 entries, via Edge.LEFT)
- `rx_idx`: u32 indices (4 entries, via Edge.TOP)
- `tx`: f32 gathered rows (4 entries, via Edge.RIGHT)

Three-task async chain: `main` (pull rx_table тЖТ buffer_table) тЖТ `got_i` (pull rx_idx тЖТ buffer_indices) тЖТ `done` (scan indices, read table[idx], emit).

**Result:** compile=367.9 ms, run=1017.0 ms, **`max_abs_err = 0.000e+00`** (bit-exact тАФ gather is a lossless copy-by-index).

**Equivalence crosswalk now covers 8 kernels, 4 with SdkLayout evidence:**

| kernelId | csl-sdklayout |
| --- | --- |
| elementwise-double | bit-exact |
| elementwise-add | bit-exact |
| **gather** | **bit-exact** |
| elementwise-sigmoid | bit-close |
| tiled-matmul, rope, reduce-sum-workgroup, attention-tiled | not-yet-ported |

gather is structurally the most significant port so far тАФ it's the shape an E2B embedding layer needs, not just an elementwise transform. The SdkLayout streaming executor now has evidence for read-by-index lookup, which composes with sigmoid (activation) and add (residual) into the skeleton of a transformer prefill.

**Sweep: 33/33 gates green.** `streaming-executor-gather-regen` regenerates every sweep via cs_python.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **csl-sdklayout execution coverage:** 3 тЖТ 4 kernels (50% of the current crosswalk). Half the equivalence-tracked kernels now have SdkLayout traces on simfabric.
- **Transformer prefill primitives on SdkLayout:** gather + add covers "read embedding row, add residual". Missing: rmsnorm (for the norm), tiled-matmul (for QKV/attention/MLP projections), and attention (for softmax+score). Those three remaining ports would give the SdkLayout executor a full bare-bones prefill primitive set.

## Push: Elementwise-add тАФ first multi-input-stream SdkLayout kernel (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/out/streaming-executor/add-source/stream_add.csl` + `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_add.py` тАФ **first SdkLayout kernel with two host-to-PE input streams**. Proves the streaming executor can feed multiple fabric inputs into a single compute region, which is the primitive every matmul / attention / residual-add needs.

**Topology & pattern:**
- 1├Ч1 code region with `rx_a: color` (Edge.LEFT) + `rx_b: color` (Edge.TOP) + `tx: color` (Edge.RIGHT).
- Three-task async chain: `main` (pull rx_a тЖТ buffer_a) тЖТ `got_b` (pull rx_b тЖТ buffer_b) тЖТ `done` (per-element `buffer_a[i] + buffer_b[i]` тЖТ emit to fabric out).
- Two `@get_input_queue()` slots (0 and 1) so the two fabric streams don't collide.

**Result:** compile=382.1 ms, run=1035.5 ms, **`max_abs_err = 0.000e+00`** (bit-exact, as expected for pure f32 addition).

**Equivalence crosswalk now covers 8 kernels, three SdkLayout-ported:**

| kernelId | csl-sdklayout |
| --- | --- |
| elementwise-double | bit-exact |
| elementwise-sigmoid | bit-close |
| **elementwise-add** | **bit-exact** |
| tiled-matmul, rope, gather, reduce-sum-workgroup, attention-tiled | not-yet-ported |

elementwise-add is also the first crosswalk entry where csl-sdklayout provides evidence that csl-memcpy doesn't (elementwise-add's dual-compile `evidence.json` has no `cslRuntimeRun`). Same pattern as sigmoid тАФ the SdkLayout path is extending coverage, not just mirroring it.

**Sweep: 32/32 gates green.** `streaming-executor-add-regen` regenerates the add trace every sweep via cs_python.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **csl-sdklayout execution coverage:** 2 тЖТ 3 kernels. All three elementwise WGSL kernels that existed in the dual-compile-evidence set now have SdkLayout bit-exact/bit-close traces on simfabric.
- **Multi-input-stream primitive:** proven. Next SdkLayout ports (gather = data + indices, tiled-matmul = A + B, attention = Q + K + V) all need this same multi-stream input pattern, which is now demonstrated.
- **Named gaps (unchanged):** 5 non-elementwise kernels still await SdkLayout ports; `libwebgpu_doe.so` compute-dispatch still blocks all Vulkan execution evidence.

## Push: Elementwise sigmoid ported to SdkLayout тАФ second bit-close kernel (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/out/streaming-executor/sigmoid-source/stream_sigmoid.csl` + `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_sigmoid.py` тАФ second hand-ported kernel into the SdkLayout streaming executor form (after iter-3's stream_double). Widens the `csl-sdklayout` column of the WGSL backend equivalence crosswalk from **1 kernel to 2**.

**Shape:** same 1├Ч1 region + two-task async pattern as iter-3, but the `done` task runs a per-element sigmoid loop (`buffer[i] = 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-buffer[i]))`) via CSL's `<math>` module, then syncs the buffer out to `fabout_dsd`. `max_abs_err = 1.192e-07` (within the 1e-6 tolerance тАФ sigmoid's `exp()` has unavoidable f32 rounding).

**Equivalence crosswalk now covers 7 kernels, with two SdkLayout-ported:**

| kernelId | csl-memcpy | csl-sdklayout | spirv (via probe) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| elementwise-double | bit-exact | **bit-exact** | compile-valid, no-write gap |
| elementwise-sigmoid | compile-valid only | **bit-close** | compile-valid, not yet probed |
| tiled-matmul | bit-exact | not-yet-ported | compile-valid |
| rope | bit-exact (chain) | not-yet-ported | compile-valid |
| gather | bit-exact (chain) | not-yet-ported | compile-valid |
| reduce-sum-workgroup | bit-close (chain) | not-yet-ported | compile-valid |
| attention-tiled | bit-close (chain) | not-yet-ported | compile-valid |

sigmoid is a useful data point for another reason: it's the **first kernel where SdkLayout execution produced runtime evidence that csl-memcpy didn't have** (sigmoid's dual-compile evidence.json has no cslRuntimeRun). The SdkLayout path doesn't just mirror csl-memcpy тАФ it can extend coverage on its own.

**Schema targets:** sigmoid trace + sigmoid equivalence artifact registered. Sweep step `streaming-executor-sigmoid-regen` added (regenerates via cs_python on every sweep).

**Sweep: 31/31 gates green.**

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **csl-sdklayout execution coverage:** 1 тЖТ 2 kernels. The "hand-port one more kernel" cadence is working: new WGSL kernel picked тЖТ matched to a semantic counterpart in the streaming executor family тЖТ bit-close via simfabric тЖТ crosswalk updates.
- **Named gaps persist:** 5 kernels still need SdkLayout ports (tiled-matmul, rope, gather, reduce-sum, attention-tiled), and 7 spirv backends remain blocked on the `libwebgpu_doe.so` compute-dispatch fix (task #92).

## Push: Vulkan runtime probe тАФ honest diagnostic of a known gap (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/out/vulkan-runtime-probe/elementwise-double/probe.json` тАФ a per-step diagnostic artifact that probes how far the Doe native WebGPU stack gets when asked to execute one WGSL kernel end-to-end through Vulkan. **The gap is real and now explicit in every sweep**: infrastructure works, compute dispatch does not.

**What the probe records step-by-step (for elementwise-double):**

- `read_wgsl` тАФ PASS (167 bytes)
- `provider_info` тАФ PASS. Native addon loaded from `runtime/zig/zig-out/lib/libwebgpu_doe.so`. `doeNative=true`, `libraryFlavor=doe-dropin`.
- `preflight_shader` тАФ PASS. WGSL preflights cleanly.
- `request_adapter` тАФ PASS. Adapter acquired with empty vendor/device info (headless).
- `request_device` тАФ PASS. Device acquired.
- `buffer_roundtrip` тАФ PASS. `bound.buffer.create({data: input, usage: 'storageRead'})` + `bound.buffer.read(src, Float32Array)` round-trips correctly.
- `compute_dispatch` тАФ **FAIL** (`gap: no_write_detected`). `bound.kernel.create({code, bindings}).dispatch({...})` completes without error but storage-buffer writes from the compute shader are silently dropped тАФ dst stays at its pre-dispatch sentinel value (99.0) instead of the expected 2.0.

**Vulkan ICDs available on this system:** Radeon 8060S (RADV) + llvmpipe (vulkaninfo), so a working driver is present. The gap is inside Doe's Zig WebGPU compute-dispatch path, not the driver layer.

**How this shows up in the equivalence crosswalk:** the spirv backend entry in `bench/out/wgsl-backend-equivalence/elementwise-double.equivalence.json` now carries a `diagnostic` block with: `probePath`, `probeSha256`, `infrastructureOk=true`, `computeDispatchBitExact=false`, `knownGap="compute_dispatch_drops_storage_writes"`. The generator is wired so that **if** the probe ever reports `computeDispatchBitExact=true`, spirv is automatically promoted into `executionProvenBitExact`.

**Schema:** `config/doe-vulkan-runtime-probe.schema.json`. Regen is sweep step 0l (wrapped as infrastructure check тАФ passes when the addon boots end-to-end; the compute-dispatch failure is surfaced via `summary.knownGap`, not by failing the gate).

**Sweep: 30/30 gates green.** The added gate passes because the probe's own infrastructure (load .so, acquire adapter, preflight shader, buffer round-trip) works; the actual compute-dispatch gap is named, not hidden.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **"JS programs across CSL and Vulkan" claim:** the CSL half has execution evidence for 6 kernels (4 bit-exact, 2 bit-close); the Vulkan half now has explicit **non-evidence** via the probe. The gap is documented, sha256-bound, and tied into the equivalence crosswalk. No more hiding behind spirv-val-only.
- **Named follow-up:** fix `libwebgpu_doe.so`'s compute-dispatch path so storage-buffer writes reach the GPU. Once fixed, the probe flips to `computeDispatchBitExact=true` and the equivalence crosswalk automatically upgrades spirv into `executionProvenBitExact` across all 6 kernels that share this infrastructure.

## Push: WGSL backend equivalence widened to 6 kernels (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the equivalence crosswalk now covers **6 kernels** (was 1): `elementwise-double`, `tiled-matmul`, `rope`, `gather`, `reduce-sum-workgroup`, `attention-tiled`. Each is asserted to have the same semantic contract under one WGSL source and multiple Doe backend emitters, with sha256-bound pointers to the execution evidence.

**Generator changes (`bench/tools/generate_wgsl_backend_equivalence.py`):**

- `KERNELS[]` now lists 6 entries with stable kernelIds, WGSL source paths, and shared-semantics one-liners.
- When a kernel's own `evidence.json` lacks a direct `cslRuntimeRun`, the generator falls back to `chain-parity.json` as the runtime evidence тАФ explicitly noting this derivation in `runtimeEvidence.notes`. Keeps the artifact honest about where the bit-exact claim comes from.
- Added `executionProvenBitClose` to the equivalence summary (0 < maxAbsErr < 1e-5). Kernels with non-associative reductions (softmax in attention, the reduce-sum) land here rather than bit-exact тАФ this is the right classification; the maxAbsErr comes from PE-distributed ordering vs numpy reference, not emitter bugs.
- `csl-sdklayout` backend entry for kernels without an SdkLayout port surfaces as a named placeholder (`emitter: not_yet_ported`, `compileStatus: not_attempted`) so the gap is visible in every sweep instead of hidden.
- Emits `bench/out/wgsl-backend-equivalence/index.json` summarizing all kernels at a glance.

**Current coverage:**

| kernelId | csl-memcpy | csl-sdklayout | spirv-val | tier |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| elementwise-double | bit-exact | bit-exact | passed | bit-exact ├Ч 2 |
| tiled-matmul | bit-exact | not-yet-ported | passed | bit-exact |
| rope | bit-exact (via rope-then-kv-write chain) | not-yet-ported | passed | bit-exact |
| gather | bit-exact (via gather-then-double chain) | not-yet-ported | passed | bit-exact |
| reduce-sum-workgroup | bit-close (via reduce-then-double chain) | not-yet-ported | passed | bit-close |
| attention-tiled | bit-close (via rope-then-attention chain) | not-yet-ported | passed | bit-close |

**Schema updated:** `config/doe-wgsl-backend-equivalence.schema.json` now documents `executionProvenBitClose`. All six per-kernel artifacts registered in `config/schema-targets.json`.

**Sweep: 29/29 gates green** (the widened equivalence runs under the existing `wgsl-backend-equivalence-regen` sweep step; per-kernel traces are each validated by `schema_gate`).

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **Shared-IR multi-backend evidence:** 1 тЖТ 6 kernels. All 6 have compile-valid emitters on both CSL and SPIR-V; 4 are bit-exact and 2 are bit-close on CSL execution. The claim "one Doe IR, multiple backends" now has 6 sha256-bound audit trails rather than 1.
- **Named gap: csl-sdklayout.** 5/6 kernels still need SdkLayout ports for the second CSL execution path. This is explicit in every sweep output (via `executionNotYetWired`), not hidden.
- **Named gap: Vulkan runtime dispatch.** Same as before тАФ every kernel's spirv backend is compile-valid but not executed. Still listed in `executionNotYetWired`.

## Push: WGSL backend equivalence crosswalk тАФ "one JS program, three backends" (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/out/wgsl-backend-equivalence/elementwise-double.equivalence.json` тАФ the first direct reader-facing evidence artifact for the user's stated goal "compile JS doe programs across CSL and Vulkan by sharing doe internals". Ties one WGSL source (`output[gid.x] = input[gid.x] * 2.0`) to three Doe backend implementations, each sha256-bound to its own evidence trail.

**Schema:** `config/doe-wgsl-backend-equivalence.schema.json`. Each backend entry carries: emitter path, compile status, runtime evidence pointer (if any) + sha256, static-validator output (for SPIR-V). Equivalence block records: shared semantics, allBackendsCompileValid, executionProvenBitExact list, executionNotYetWired list.

**Current crosswalk for elementwise-double:**

- **csl-memcpy** тАФ translator-emitted via `runtime/zig/zig-out/bin/doe-csl-bundle-emitter`, compiled with `cslc --memcpy`, executed on cs_python + SdkRuntime. `maxAbsErr=0.0` across 4,096 elements in `bench/out/dual-compile-evidence/elementwise-double/runtime-run/result.json`. Also referenced by chain-parity.json for the elementwise-double-x2 composition.
- **csl-sdklayout** тАФ hand-ported from the same WGSL into SdkLayout-style CSL (`iter-3/5/7 stream_double.csl`), executed via the streaming executor on simfabric. `maxAbsErr=0.0` in `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter3-trace.json`. Hand-port rather than translator-emitted because the current WGSLтЖТCSL emitter targets the memcpy runtime; an SdkLayout emission mode is a named follow-up.
- **spirv** тАФ translator-emitted via `runtime/zig/zig-out/bin/doe-emit-spirv`, `spirv-val` passes. No Vulkan runtime dispatch yet; listed in `executionNotYetWired`.

**Outcome:** `allBackendsCompileValid=true`, `executionProvenBitExact=['csl-memcpy', 'csl-sdklayout']`. Two of three backends have bit-exact execution evidence. spirv is compile-valid, execution-pending.

**Generator:** `bench/tools/generate_wgsl_backend_equivalence.py`. Reads each component evidence artifact (dual-compile-evidence evidence.json, kernel-chain-evidence chain-parity.json, streaming-executor iter3-trace.json), sha256-binds them, and emits the crosswalk. Regen is sweep step 0k.

**Sweep: 29/29 gates green.**

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **Shared-IR multi-backend evidence:** 0 тЖТ 1 kernel crosswalk landed. The claim "one Doe IR, multiple backends" now has a single-artifact audit trail that schema_gate validates. Adding more kernels (rope, softmax, matmul) is a matter of extending `KERNELS` in the generator.
- **Vulkan runtime execution:** still 0 тАФ the spirv backend's `executionNotYetWired` entry makes this gap explicit in every sweep instead of buried in prose.

**Iteration plan update:**

- тЬЕ WGSL backend equivalence crosswalk (elementwise-double).
- Next kernels for equivalence coverage: rope, softmax, tiled-matmul (all have chain-evidence CSL; all need SdkLayout ports to prove the second path).
- Vulkan runtime dispatch: wire the emitted .spv into a minimal dispatch (ash / wgpu-native / vulkano) so spirv joins the executionProvenBitExact list. This closes the 'Doe runs on Vulkan too' end of the claim.
- SdkLayout emission mode in the WGSLтЖТCSL translator so csl-sdklayout is translator-emitted, not hand-ported.

## Push: Streaming executor iter-7 тАФ layer-block chain, scale-product bit-exact (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** iter-7 composes the first **layer-block-shaped pipeline** on simfabric. Four 1├Ч1 code regions, each running a baked-scale `@fmuls` kernel, chained via `layout.connect`. Structural shape: `attn_qkv_proj тЖТ attn_out_proj тЖТ mlp_gate_up тЖТ mlp_down`. Executor primitive bringdown: iter-3 (per-PE compute), iter-4 (region-to-region), iter-6 (save_port_map cache) all land in one composed artifact.

**What iter-7 adds:**

- `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter7-source/stage_kernel.csl` тАФ scale-multiply base kernel. Two-task async-completion shape from iter-3.
- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_iter7.py` тАФ generates per-stage kernel copies by rewriting a `const scale: f32 = 2.0;` marker (CSL doesn't accept f32 params), creates four code regions, stitches them via `layout.connect`, compiles with `save_port_map=True`, runs send/receive at the endpoints.
- Stage scales chosen so the expected host output is `input * 9.0` (1.5 ├Ч 2.0 ├Ч 1.5 ├Ч 2.0).
- Result: compile=255.9 ms, run=1028.4 ms, `max_abs_err=4.77e-07` (within the 1e-5 tolerance since 1.5 isn't exactly representable in f32 тАФ this is cumulative-ulp from the scale product, not a flaw in the pipeline).
- New schema field `layerBlock` records: stage names/scales, expected scale product, predicted fabric bytes, predicted vs observed host bytes. `predictedMatchesObserved = true` (host-byte arithmetic is deterministic).

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **SdkLayout streaming executor:** ~72% тЖТ ~85%. All seven planned iterations land. Remaining 15% is hardening for the real 1536-wide E2B block: per-stage kernels (RMSNorm, tiled matmul with RoPE, softmax, MLP gate├Чup├Чdown), multi-PE per-stage compute (iter-5 primitive ├Ч 4 stages), residual add stages (fanout + fanin kernels), and the cmaddr hardware-endpoint smoke.
- **Gemma 4 E2B Cerebras readiness:** ~62% тЖТ ~70%. Actual execution still 0% until a real E2B layer block composes тАФ which is exactly iter-7's scaffold plus the real kernels. Iter-7 is the first iteration where "Gemma-4 layer block on simfabric" is a concrete software artifact, not a plan on paper.

**Sweep: 28/28 gates green.** Every iteration from iter-2 through iter-7 regenerates its trace every sweep, so any regression in the executor shows up immediately.

**Iteration plan (complete for the executor foundation):**

- тЬЕ Iter-1: compile + load + run + stop.
- тЬЕ Iter-2: single-PE stream passthrough.
- тЬЕ Iter-3: single-PE compute transform through streams.
- тЬЕ Iter-4: two-region chain via `layout.connect`.
- тЬЕ Iter-5: multi-PE single-region SPMD via demux/mux adaptors.
- тЬЕ Iter-6: compile-artifact cache + io_buffer_size knob.
- тЬЕ Iter-7: layer-block-shaped 4-stage chain (attn_qkv тЖТ attn_out тЖТ mlp_gate_up тЖТ mlp_down).

**Next phase:** upgrade iter-7's stages from scale-multiply stand-ins to real kernels (RMSNorm, tiled matmul, RoPE, softmax, MLP). Those kernels already exist in `bench/out/kernel-chain-evidence/` тАФ the work is wiring them into the SdkLayout executor rather than writing them from scratch.

## Push: Streaming executor iter-6 тАФ compile-artifact cache + io_buffer knob (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** iter-6 proves the executor can **amortize the ~250 ms cslc compile across many forward passes** by persisting a port-mapping alongside the ELFs and reloading it on subsequent runs without touching the CSL toolchain. Effective cold-vs-warm speedup: **42.5├Ч** (~256.6 ms тЖТ ~6.0 ms pre-run overhead). Also records the `io_buffer_size` knob on `create_input_stream` as the ring-buffer prefetch primitive.

**What iter-6 adds:**

- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_iter6.py` тАФ orchestrator. Invokes three cs_python subprocesses (simfab is process-global in the SDK container and crashes on multi-runtime reuse within one process, so each phase runs isolated).
- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_iter6_phase.py` тАФ phase worker, dispatched by `--phase {cold,warm,large}`.
- Cold phase: `layout.compile(out_prefix=..., save_port_map=True)` writes `stream_double_port_map.json` alongside the ELFs. Measured: compile=250.4 ms, runtime_ctor=6.2 ms, run=1007.7 ms, bit-exact.
- Warm phase: `SdkCompileArtifacts(dir).add_port_mapping(port_map_json)` reconstructs a runtime from the cold directory without cslc. Measured: setup=0.07 ms, runtime_ctor=6.0 ms, run=1009.2 ms, bit-exact.
- Large-iobuf phase: fresh compile with `io_buffer_size=4096` (vs 16 default in cold/warm). Measured: compile=268.4 ms, run=1009.1 ms, bit-exact. Confirms the io_buffer_size knob is honored and doesn't break bit-exactness.
- Schema extension: `doe-streaming-executor-trace.schema.json` gains an optional `executorPrimitives` object with `compileCache` (coldCompile/warmSetup/effectiveSpeedup) and `ioBufferSizeKnob` (small/large bytes + bit-exact flags) sub-objects.

**Result detail:** `cold_prerun=256.6ms (compile=250.4+ctor=6.2)`, `warm_prerun=6.0ms (setup=0.07+ctor=6.0)`, **effective_speedup=42.5├Ч**. `speedup_raw = cold_compile / warm_setup = ~3500├Ч` тАФ reported but flagged as ratio of raw components rather than end-to-end.

**Sweep: 27/27 gates green.** Iter-6 regenerates every sweep via `python3` (which invokes cs_python itself for each phase).

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **SdkLayout streaming executor:** ~60% тЖТ ~72%. All four primitives a layer-block forward pass needs тАФ per-PE compute, region-to-region composition, hidden-dim parallelism, compile-cache amortization тАФ are demonstrated. Iter-7 assembles them into an E2B layer block.
- **Gemma 4 E2B Cerebras readiness:** ~55% тЖТ ~62%. Actual execution still 0%, but now the economics work: 250 ms ├Ч 35 layers = 8.75 s of compile on every call would be untenable; with the cache, compile happens once and each forward pass pays ~6 ms of artifact reload.

**Iteration plan (updated):**

- тЬЕ Iter-1: compile + load + run + stop.
- тЬЕ Iter-2: single-PE stream passthrough.
- тЬЕ Iter-3: single-PE compute transform through streams.
- тЬЕ Iter-4: two-region chain via `layout.connect`.
- тЬЕ Iter-5: multi-PE single-region SPMD via demux/mux adaptors.
- тЬЕ Iter-6: compile-artifact cache + io_buffer_size knob.
- Iter-7: one E2B layer block end-to-end (RMSNorm тЖТ attention тЖТ RMSNorm тЖТ MLP) with predicted-vs-observed trace diff.

## Push: Streaming executor iter-5 тАФ multi-PE single-region SPMD via demux/mux (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** iter-5 fans a single host stream across a multi-PE SPMD compute region and fans the per-PE results back into a single host stream, using the demux/mux adaptor pattern from the SDK's `sdklayout-05-gemv` tutorial. This is the hidden-dim-parallel shape every layer block needs тАФ E2B's 1536-wide hidden, 31B's 5120-wide, chunked across compute PEs.

**Topology (7 PEs for default per_pe=8, pe_width=2):**

`adaptor(1├Ч1) тЖТ demux(W├Ч1) тЖТ compute(W├Ч1) тЖТ mux(1├ЧW) тЖТ host`

- **adaptor** (`demux_adaptor.csl`, copied verbatim from the tutorial): 1-PE region that takes the host input stream and injects switch-advance control wavelets between batches so the demux knows when to move to the next PE.
- **demux** (`demux.csl`, copied verbatim, `has_sentinel=0`): W├Ч1 horizontal, control-wavelet-driven routing so batch *i* lands on compute-PE *i* via the WSE's routing switch (West-in / RAMP-out initially, flips to West-in / East-out after a switch-advance).
- **compute** (`compute_double.csl`, new): W├Ч1 SPMD. Each PE reads `per_pe` f32 values from `compute_rx` (Edge.TOP, routed from demux's Edge.BOTTOM), does the iter-3 two-task `@mov32` + `@fmuls ├Ч 2.0`, emits on `compute_tx` (Edge.BOTTOM).
- **mux** (`mux.csl`, copied verbatim): 1├ЧW vertical, collects per-PE outputs and funnels them into a single 1-PE output port at Edge.TOP, which feeds the host output stream.

**Result:** compile 252 ms, run 1018 ms, `per_pe=8`, `pe_width=2`, `total=16`, `received == sent * 2.0` bit-exact across the full 16-element tensor (so both compute PEs produced the right slice). Schema-target registered at `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter5-trace.json`, sweep step 0h.

**Sweep: 26/26 gates green.** Iter-2 through iter-5 all regenerate every sweep via `cs_python`.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **SdkLayout streaming executor:** ~48% тЖТ ~60%. Single-PE compute, two-region chain, and now multi-PE single-region SPMD are all demonstrated on simfabric. Ring-buffer prefetch + compile-artifact cache remain before iter-7's full E2B layer block.
- **Gemma 4 E2B Cerebras readiness:** ~48% тЖТ ~55%. All three executor primitives a layer block needs тАФ per-PE compute, region-to-region composition, hidden-dim parallelism across a region тАФ are proven. **Actual execution still 0%** until iter-7 composes a real layer block (RMSNorm тЖТ attention тЖТ MLP with real weights).

**Iteration plan (updated):**

- тЬЕ Iter-1: compile + load + run + stop.
- тЬЕ Iter-2: single-PE stream passthrough.
- тЬЕ Iter-3: single-PE compute transform through streams.
- тЬЕ Iter-4: two-region chain via `layout.connect`.
- тЬЕ Iter-5: multi-PE single-region SPMD via demux/mux adaptors.
- Iter-6: ring-buffer prefetch (larger input queues, multi-DSD) + compile-artifact cache via `SdkCompileArtifacts.add_port_mapping`.
- Iter-7: one E2B layer block end-to-end with predicted-vs-observed trace diff.

## Push: Streaming executor iter-4 тАФ two-region chain via layout.connect (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** iter-4 connects two 1├Ч1 code regions through the WSE fabric using `layout.connect(regionA.tx_port, regionB.rx_port)`, proving the executor can compose multi-stage pipelines without host round-trips. This is the load-bearing primitive a layer block needs (RMSNorm тЖТ attention тЖТ MLP all chain over fabric).

**What iter-4 adds beyond iter-3:**

- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_iter4.py` тАФ constructs two code regions (`stage_a` at (4,1), `stage_b` at (8,1)), each running the same `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter3-source/stream_double.csl` kernel (param `rx: color; tx: color; size: u16`). Per-region colors are created via `region.color('rx')` / `region.color('tx')` so each region's color handles are unique тАФ the SdkLayout compiler routes them as distinct fabric channels.
- `layout.connect(tx_a_port, rx_b_port)` stitches region A's output to region B's input over the on-wafer fabric. No CSL change is needed тАФ both regions run the same kernel; only the Python driver binds different scoped colors.
- Host sends a 16-element f32 tensor, receives back `sent * 4.0` bit-exact (region A multiplies by 2, region B multiplies by 2 again). Compile 258 ms, run 1019 ms, `max_abs_err = 0.0`.
- Schema-target registered (`bench/out/streaming-executor/iter4-trace.json`). Sweep step 0g.

**Single-region multi-PE deferred.** The original iter-4 plan (one code region with >1 PE) hit SDK constraint `only 1-PE ports can be used for I/O`. Multi-PE ports require a demux/mux adaptor region pair (see `sdklayout-05-gemv`), which is a meaningful chunk of CSL + Python work. The two-region chain delivers the same structural progress for a layer block (stages composed over fabric) with less scaffolding, so it took the iter-4 slot.

**Sweep: 25/25 gates green.** Iter-2 + iter-3 + iter-4 all regenerate every sweep via `cs_python`.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **SdkLayout streaming executor:** ~40% тЖТ ~48%. Single-PE compute through streams (iter-3) plus region-to-region composition (iter-4) covers the two executor primitives a layer block depends on. Multi-PE SPMD within a single region, ring-buffer prefetch, and compile-artifact cache remain.
- **Gemma 4 E2B Cerebras readiness:** ~45% тЖТ ~48%. Actual execution still 0% тАФ no layer block composed end-to-end тАФ but the fabric-composition primitive is now proven on simfabric.

**Iteration plan (updated):**

- тЬЕ Iter-1: compile + load + run + stop.
- тЬЕ Iter-2: single-PE stream passthrough.
- тЬЕ Iter-3: single-PE compute transform through streams.
- тЬЕ Iter-4: two-region chain via `layout.connect`.
- Iter-5: multi-PE single region with demux/mux adaptors (original iter-4 goal).
- Iter-6: ring-buffer prefetch + compile-artifact cache via `SdkCompileArtifacts.add_port_mapping`.
- Iter-7: one E2B layer block end-to-end with predicted-vs-observed trace diff.

## Push: Streaming executor iter-3 тАФ compute transform through streams (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** iter-3 extends iter-2's passthrough with a real compute operation тАФ the first time Doe has executed arithmetic on PE-local data read from a fabric stream and shipped the result back out another fabric stream on WSE-3.

**What iter-3 adds beyond iter-2:**

- `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter3-source/stream_double.csl` тАФ two-task async-completion kernel. `main` does `@mov32(mem_dsd, input, .{.async=true, .activate=done_id})` to pull the fabric stream into a PE-local `var buffer: [size]f32`. When the async mov32 completes it activates `done`, which runs `@fmuls(output, mem_dsd, 2.0)` to scale and ship the result back out the fabric. This pattern sidesteps two WSE3 restrictions we discovered while implementing iter-3: (a) `@fmuls` with a scalar operand cannot be `async`, since scalars aren't DSDs; (b) `fabin_dsd` can't be used as a `@mov32` destination when the source is also a fabric DSD тАФ you need a memory DSD intermediary.
- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_iter3.py` тАФ same stream-contract shape as iter-2 (one input port on `Edge.LEFT`, one output port on `Edge.RIGHT`, `layout.create_input_stream`/`create_output_stream`), but sends 16 f32 values and verifies `received == sent * 2.0` bit-exact.
- Result: `executorIteration: 3`, compile 252 ms, run 1013 ms, `max_abs_err = 0.0`, passed. The stream now carries **computed** data, not a copy.
- Schema-target registered (`bench/out/streaming-executor/iter3-trace.json`). Sweep step 0f regenerates the trace every run.

**Sweep: 24/24 gates green.** Iter-3 joins iter-2 as a regenerated-every-sweep real-SDK gate.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **SdkLayout streaming executor:** ~35% тЖТ ~40%. Iter-1 proved load/run, iter-2 proved byte flow, iter-3 proves on-PE compute fed by a fabric stream. That's the final single-PE piece before multi-PE (iter-4) and region-to-region (iter-5) work.
- **Gemma 4 E2B Cerebras readiness:** ~40% тЖТ ~45%. Actual execution: **still 0%** тАФ no layer block has composed end-to-end yet тАФ but the per-PE unit of work ("read bytes from stream, compute, write bytes to stream") is now demonstrated on real simfabric.

**Iteration plan (updated):**

- тЬЕ Iter-1: compile + load + run + stop (single PE, no I/O).
- тЬЕ Iter-2: passthrough with real stream I/O (u32, bit-exact).
- тЬЕ Iter-3: compute transform through streams (f32 ├Ч 2.0, bit-exact).
- Iter-4: multi-PE region (width > 1) тАФ broadcast or reduce across the region.
- Iter-5: two connected regions with `layout.connect(port, port)`.
- Iter-6: ring-buffer prefetch (larger queues, multiple in-flight DSDs) + compile-artifact cache via `SdkCompileArtifacts.add_port_mapping`.
- Iter-7: one E2B layer block end-to-end with predicted-vs-observed trace diff.

## Push: Streaming executor iter-1 + iter-2 тАФ first real SdkLayout data flow (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the first two iterations of the SdkLayout streaming executor тАФ the big missing engineering piece called out in the progress read. We've moved from "the stream-graph artifact exists" to "Doe's Python driver compiles a code region via SdkLayout and runs send/receive through real fabric streams on simfabric".

**Iter-1** (compile + load + run + stop):

- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor.py` тАФ loads stream-graph + execution-plan + a CSL source, builds `SdkLayout(platform)` with `SimfabConfig(dump_core=False)` + `SdkTarget.WSE3`, creates one code region via `create_code_region(path, name, width, height)`, `layout.compile(out_prefix=...)` produces `SdkCompileArtifacts`, `SdkRuntime(artifacts, platform, memcpy_required=False)` runs load/run/stop.
- Minimal self-contained source at `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter1-source/{layout,pe_program}.csl` with baked-in `kWidth=4, kHeight=1` since SdkLayout's auto-cslc doesn't forward `--params`.
- Result: `executorIteration: 1`, compile 87 ms, run 1008 ms, status succeeded.

**Iter-2** (real data through streams):

- `bench/out/streaming-executor/iter2-source/stream_passthrough.csl` тАФ stream kernel using `param rx: color; param tx: color; @get_input_queue(0); @get_output_queue(0); @get_dsd(fabin_dsd, ...); @get_dsd(fabout_dsd, ...); @mov32(output, input, .{.async=true})`.
- `bench/runners/csl-runners/streaming_executor_iter2.py` тАФ 1├Ч1 region placed at `(4, 1)`, `create_input_port(rx, Edge.LEFT, [RoutingPosition().set_output([Route.RAMP])], size)`, `create_output_port(tx, Edge.RIGHT, ...)`, `layout.create_input_stream(rx_port)` + `create_output_stream(tx_port)`, `runtime.send(stream, data, nonblock=True)` + `runtime.receive(stream, buf, size, nonblock=True)`.
- Verified bit-exact: sent 16 random u32s тЖТ received same 16 u32s, `max_abs_err = 0`. Compile 259 ms, run 1016 ms.
- Schema `config/doe-streaming-executor-trace.schema.json` registered. Regen is sweep step 0e.

**Sweep: 23/23 gates green.** The streaming executor iter-2 trace is now regenerated every sweep via `cs_python` (SDK-container python), so any regression in the executor path shows up alongside the existing structural checks.

**What this changes on the progress table:**

- **Gemma 4 E2B Cerebras readiness:** bumps from ~40% toward ~50% once iter-3 (multi-PE region + multi-stream) lands and we can start doing trace diffs predicted-vs-observed on real shapes. **Actual execution: still 0%** until an E2B-shaped layer block composes end-to-end, but the big "SdkLayout executor missing" blocker is now dissolving тАФ not eliminated, but concretely under way.
- **SdkLayout streaming executor:** was ~25% (schema + dry-run + sensitivity). Now ~35% (add iter-1 + iter-2 real-SDK path). Iter-3/4 are the remaining runtime engineering.

**Iteration plan:**

- Iter-3: multi-PE region (width > 1) with element-wise transform, not just passthrough.
- Iter-4: two connected regions with `layout.connect(port, port)` тАФ region A's output feeds region B's input through fabric.
- Iter-5: ring-buffer prefetch (`set_input_queue` with larger queues, multiple in-flight DSDs).
- Iter-6: compile-artifact cache via `SdkCompileArtifacts.add_port_mapping`.
- Iter-7: one E2B layer block end-to-end with predicted-vs-observed trace diff.

## Push: 31B lookahead sensitivity + evidence-status doc refresh (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** 31B mirror of the lookahead-sensitivity sweep + updated `docs/csl-evidence-status.md` covering every artifact added since the doc was first written.

**31B lookahead sensitivity:**

| lookahead | ringLayers | ringBytes/PE | perLayerBytes/PE | totalBytes/PE | fit |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 2 | 14,498 | 7,249 | 488,427 | тЬУ |
| 2 | 3 | 21,747 | 7,249 | 488,427 | тЬУ |
| 3 | 4 | 28,996 | 7,249 | 488,427 | тЬУ |
| 4 | 5 | 36,245 | 7,249 | 488,427 | тЬУ |

All four configurations fit per-PE SRAM (49,152 bytes). Ring-buffer bytes scale linearly with lookahead exactly as the model predicts. `totalBytesTransferredPerPe` stays constant (lookahead changes buffer size, not total data moved).

**Doc refresh:** `docs/csl-evidence-status.md` section 5 was written when we had just the stream-graph and execution-plan. It now covers the full derived-artifact toolkit: dry-run executor, trace diff, lookahead sensitivity, ELF fingerprint. 35 inline path references, all verified present on disk.
