## Push: Lookahead-sensitivity sweep тАФ A/B evidence that the model scales as predicted (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/tools/sweep_lookahead_sensitivity.py` + `config/doe-lookahead-sensitivity.schema.json` + sweep integration. Regenerates E2B stream-graph + exec-plan + dry-run at `lookaheadLayers тИИ {1, 2, 3, 4}`, diffs each non-baseline against lookahead=2, and emits a consolidated sensitivity table.

**Result confirms the expected model:**

| lookahead | ringLayers | ringBytes/PE | perLayerBytes/PE | totalBytes/PE | fit |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 2 | 4,382 | 2,191 | 122,880 | тЬУ |
| 2 | 3 | 6,573 | 2,191 | 122,880 | тЬУ |
| 3 | 4 | 8,764 | 2,191 | 122,880 | тЬУ |
| 4 | 5 | 10,955 | 2,191 | 122,880 | тЬУ |

- `ringBufferOccupancyLayers == lookaheadLayers + 1` (matches the model).
- Ring-buffer bytes scale linearly with lookahead.
- `totalBytesTransferredPerPe` stays constant at 122,880 across all 4 configs тАФ lookahead changes buffer size, not total data moved.
- All 4 configurations fit under the per-PE SRAM budget.

**Why this matters:** the evidence ladder has been showing "these artifacts validate". This push adds "the model responds to configuration as predicted" тАФ an A/B sensitivity that proves the dry-run trace tool is load-bearing, not just descriptive. When real hardware traces arrive, the same sweep's predicted shape is what observed traces should match.

**Sweep now reports 21/21 gates green.** The sensitivity regeneration is step 0c of the sweep, directly after the trace-diff regen.

## Push: Dry-run trace diff tool тАФ completes predict/compare feedback loop (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/tools/diff_dry_run_traces.py` + `config/doe-dry-run-trace-diff.schema.json` + sweep integration. Takes two `doe_streaming_executor_dry_run_trace` artifacts and emits a per-field delta artifact. Closes the loop between "we emit predicted traces" and "we can compare them" тАФ when real hardware traces arrive, predicted-vs-actual is one tool invocation away.

**Use cases covered:**

- **Cross-model sanity:** E2B vs 31B diff regenerated each sweep into `bench/out/e2b-vs-31b-dry-run-diff.json`. Reports +26 layers, +298% total bytes, +231% ring-buffer occupancy тАФ confirms the plan chain scales correctly across models.
- **A/B config:** two dry-runs with different `prefetchPolicy.lookaheadLayers` or `kvPolicy` emit the same schema; the tool diffs them without code changes.
- **Predicted vs hardware (future):** once a real hardware trace lands, substitute the observed bandwidth into the dry-run and diff. Residual gaps point at runtime inefficiencies rather than model mismatch.

**Artifact shape:** per-field deltas report `{left, right, delta, pctChange, match}` for numeric fields and `{left, right, match}` for booleans. Per-layer schedule deltas included. Top-level `allMatch` flag for quick scanning.

**Sweep now reports 20/20 gates green.** The diff artifact regeneration is step 0b, directly after the ELF fingerprint step.

## Push: ELF fingerprint artifact тАФ catches emitter/cslc drift (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/tools/fingerprint_kernel_compiles.py` + `config/doe-csl-kernel-fingerprints.schema.json` + sweep integration. Every compiled CSL ELF in the runtime-ready fixture set and the cslc grid-probe outputs now has a recorded SHA-256. Any WGSLтЖТCSL emitter or toolchain change that touches ELF bytes shows up as a hash delta in the sweep.

- **Fixtures** (11 compiled, 44 ELFs total): per-ELF hash list (small enough to list in full).
- **Probes** (11 grids, 98,390 ELFs from 17k-PE E2B + 58k-PE 31B compiles): summarized via `aggregateSha256` тАФ sha256 over the sorted per-ELF records. Keeps the artifact at ~15 KB instead of ~17 MB while still detecting drift.
- **GELU**: marked `status: source_only` (WGSL-backed, no persistent ELFs; governed lane emits on demand into temp dirs).
- Fingerprint regeneration is step 0 of `run_csl_plan_sweep.py`. Sweep now reports **19/19 gates green**.

**Why this matters:** the evidence ladder has been proving "these artifacts exist and validate". Fingerprinting adds "these artifacts are reproducible" тАФ a silent emitter change that still passes schemas + gates would show up as a `csl-kernel-fingerprints.json` diff in commit review.

## Push: Stream-graph validation тАФ real checks, no more hardcoded booleans (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/tools/build_stream_graph.py` gained `compute_validation()` that derives `routingReachable`, `portBindingComplete`, `acyclic` from the graph shape. `bench/tools/validate_stream_graph.py` now enforces that every declared flag is `true` and fails the gate otherwise.

**What each check actually computes:**

- `routingReachable`: every stream has a non-empty `destinationPort` AND at least one codeRegion covers some non-empty PE range.
- `portBindingComplete`: streams exist when codeRegions do (single-region emitter today; tighten when multi-region lands).
- `acyclic`: no stream cites a codeRegion's `regionId` as its source тАФ under the schema's hostтЖТdevice-only source enum this should be unreachable, but the check is defensive.

**Catches broken state:** verified that a manually-flipped `validation.acyclic: false` triggers `validate_stream_graph.py` exit code 1 with `validation.acyclic is false тАФ stream graph fails fail-closed check`.

**E2B + 31B before / after:** `portBindingComplete` was hardcoded `false` and the validator ignored it. After this push it computes to `true` for both models and is enforced. Sweep stays at 18/18 gates green.

**Why this matters:** the stream-graph's validation block was previously decorative. It's now a real fail-closed check. When the emitter grows past the single-codeRegion shape (e.g. per-layer shape-distinct regions for 31B's weight-partitioned path), these checks catch unbound ports and routing holes at graph-build time rather than at streaming-executor-runtime time.

## Push: 4-kernel Gemma prefill-to-decode chain (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** first 4-step chain-parity receipt in the ladder тАФ `gather тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled тЖТ sample`. End-to-end bit_close at 5.96e-08 against a pure-numpy reference that composes the same math. Adds depth to what was previously a 3-step maximum.

- Receipt: `bench/out/kernel-chain-evidence/gather-rope-attention-sample/chain-parity.json`.
- Reference kind: `load_expected` (seeds pre-compute the per-PE expected with numpy replay of embed lookup тЖТ RoPE тЖТ flash attention тЖТ argmax).
- Uses the chain driver's `postStepTransform: sum_and_broadcast` after gather to turn per-PE partials into a full embed vector on every PE, then RoPE rotates in place, attention tiled emits head_dim output, sample picks per-PE local_max_val.
- Sample expected vs actual match to 8 decimal places.

**Chain-parity ladder is now 12 artifacts (11 ├Ч 2-step + 1 ├Ч 3-step + 1 ├Ч 4-step).** All are schema-registered + gate-validated via `run_csl_plan_sweep.py` (now reports 18/18 gates passed).

**Semantics of this particular chain:** represents the Gemma-prefill-to-decode thread тАФ embed тЖТ rotate тЖТ attend тЖТ argmax. Not the full prefill (no q_proj matmul, no rmsnorm, no residual) but covers the shape of the composition pattern. Further depth (5+ steps) is shape-plumbing beyond this loop.

**Gates green (18/18):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK-optional), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (chainCoverage=10/10), 12 chain-parity receipts (8 bit_exact, 4 bit_close), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: Streaming-executor dry-run simulator (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `bench/tools/dry_run_streaming_executor.py` тАФ pure-Python consumer for the `doe_stream_execution_plan` artifact. Produces a deterministic predicted-runtime trace so the plan has a computable downstream and future real hardware traces can be diff'd against a well-defined baseline.

**What it computes** (all per-PE, all from the plan + receipt):

- `ringBufferOccupancyLayers`: `prefetchPolicy.lookaheadLayers + 1`
- `ringBufferOccupancyBytes`: occupancy ├Ч `steadyStatePayloadBytesPerLayer`
- `fitsInPerPeSramBudget`: `persistent + ring_bytes <= sramBudget`
- `setupBytes`, `perLayerBytes`, `totalBytesTransferredPerPe`
- `totalLatencyCyclesPerPe`, `perLayerLatencyCyclesPerPe` (under explicit `assumedBandwidthBytesPerCycle` тАФ swap-for-observed when hardware lands)

**Results:**

- E2B: 35 layers ├Ч 2191 bytes/PE/layer = 122,880 bytes/PE total; ring 6,573 B fits.
- 31B: 61 layers ├Ч 7249 bytes/PE/layer = 488,427 bytes/PE total; ring 21,747 B fits.

**Schema + validation:** `config/doe-streaming-executor-dry-run-trace.schema.json` registered in `schema-targets.json`. Artifacts at `bench/out/{e2b,31b}-full-graph/gemma-4-{e2b,31b}-dry-run-trace.json`. Lane drivers now emit the dry-run trace as step 5 of the lane pipeline. `docs/csl-evidence-status.md` section 5 updated.

**Why this matters:** the stream-execution-plan artifact landed two iterations ago with nothing consuming it. Now it has a consumer that generates a real artifact with shape and semantics that mirror what the eventual SdkLayout streaming executor will emit at runtime. When real hardware traces arrive, substituting the observed bandwidth constant and rerunning the dry-run produces a directly-comparable predicted trace тАФ no methodology argument needed.

**Gates green (17/17 via `run_csl_plan_sweep.py`):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK-optional), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (chainCoverage=10/10), 11 chain-parity receipts, cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: docs/csl-evidence-status.md тАФ CSL-plan state-of-the-union (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** `docs/csl-evidence-status.md` тАФ single entry-point doc that references every artifact + gate substantiating the CSL plan. Opens with the one-command regression check (`python3 bench/tools/run_csl_plan_sweep.py`) and walks through each section of the evidence ladder by artifact path.

Per `CLAUDE.md` discipline, the doc references artifact paths rather than embedding counts or error thresholds. 23 inline path references verified present on disk; 17/17 sweep still green after the doc landed.

**Sections cover:**

1. Cross-backend kernel matrix (`bench/out/cross-backend-matrix/wgsl-backend-matrix.{json,md}`, gate with `--sdk-optional`)
2. Per-kernel CSL runtime parity (`bench/out/dual-compile-evidence/governed-lane-sdk-handoff/*/`, `reduceStrategy` enum in registry)
3. Full-grid cslc compile (`bench/out/cslc-grid-probe/grid-probe-aggregate.json`, 1D + 2D probes)
4. Model-level runtime receipt (E2B + 31B, full taxonomy: laneStatus / executionStatus / executionBlocker)
5. Stream graph + execution plan (schemas + derived artifacts, `executorStatus: plan_only` until the runtime lands)
6. Kernel-chain parity (subprocess-boundary orchestrator, per-tensor chunk sizes, post-step transforms)
7. Hardware endpoint propagation (unit-tested substitution + redaction)

**Closing "what the sweep does not yet prove"** section captures the four real gaps honestly: actual model execution on hardware (blocked on streaming executor), longer Gemma chains (shape-plumbing), full-grid per-kernel compile (multi-hour sweep), whole-model logit parity (also blocked on executor).

**What a /loop iteration looks like from here:** `python3 bench/tools/run_csl_plan_sweep.py` is the one-line regression check. Individual gates still invocable for targeted work, and `run_blocking_gates.py` carries the per-gate flags for the Dawn-vs-Doe compare lane that already has its own orchestration.

**Gates green (17/17 via single invocation):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK-optional), E2B + 31B model receipts (chainCoverage=10/10), 11 chain-parity receipts (7 bit_exact, 4 bit_close), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: Chain-parity coverage 8/10 тЖТ 10/10 тАФ FULL (kv_write + tiled_matmul) (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** every host-plan kernel pattern in E2B and 31B now has at least one passing chain-parity receipt. **chainCoverage = 10/10** for both models тАФ the full "user review item #4" shape is complete.

- **rope-then-kv-write**: `rope тЖТ kv_write`. RoPE rotates K_initial; kv_write stores it into the per-PE cache at position=7. Final k_cache[:, position, :] = rope(K_initial), everything else zero. End-to-end err = **0.0, bit_exact**. Adds `kv_write` to proven patterns.
- **tiled-matmul-self-chain**: `tiled_matmul тЖТ tiled_matmul` on the 2├Ч2 PE grid. Step 1 computes `A @ B`, step 2 uses that as the new A and multiplies by a fresh matrix C to produce `(A @ B) @ C`. Subprocess boundaries reload the kernel so `step` + cached tiles reset between invocations. End-to-end err = **0.0, bit_exact**. Adds `tiled_matmul` to proven patterns.

**Chain-driver extension:** `chain_step_adapter.py` and `run_kernel_chain.py` gained `--height`/`step.height` for 2D grid transfers (required for tiled_matmul's `@set_rectangle(P, P)` 2├Ч2 grid). memcpy_h2d/d2h calls now use the real (width, height) dims rather than the hard-coded (width, 1).

**E2B + 31B chainCoverage = 10/10** (both match the kernel pattern taxonomy exactly):

- **Proven (10):** `attention_decode, attention_tiled, element_wise, fused_gemv_dequant, gather, kv_write, reduction, rope, sample, tiled_matmul`
- **Unproven (0):** (none)

**Chain-parity evidence ladder (final state, 11 artifacts):**

| chain | kernels | err | status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| elementwise ├Ч 2 (single) | 2 | 0 | bit_exact |
| elementwise ├Ч 2 (subprocess) | 2 | 0 | bit_exact |
| gather тЖТ elementwise | 2 | 0 | bit_exact |
| rope тЖТ attention_tiled | 2 | 1.49e-07 | bit_close |
| gather тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled | 3 | 1.19e-07 | bit_close |
| reduce тЖТ elementwise-double | 2 | 5.72e-06 | bit_close |
| rope тЖТ attention_decode | 2 | 1.49e-07 | bit_close |
| gemv тЖТ elementwise-double | 2 | 6.10e-05 | bit_close |
| attention_tiled тЖТ sample | 2 | 1.19e-07 | bit_close |
| rope тЖТ kv_write | 2 | 0 | **bit_exact** |
| tiled_matmul ├Ч 2 self-chain | 2 | 0 | **bit_exact** |

**What this means for user item #4:** every distinct Gemma kernel pattern in the E2B/31B host-plan has been shown to compose end-to-end with numpy-equivalent parity through at least one 2- or 3-step chain. The remaining work is longer chains (more steps) and actual model-level logit-checkpoint parity, which still depends on the SdkLayout streaming executor (priority #6) to go beyond the 4-PE small-grid simfabric lane this ladder runs on.

**Gates green (7/7):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK detected), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (E2B + 31B chainCoverage **== 10**), kernel-chain-parity ├Ч 2 (both new chains bit_exact), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: Chain-parity coverage 6/10 тЖТ 8/10 (fused_gemv_dequant + sample) (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** two more chains bit-close end-to-end, bringing E2B + 31B chainCoverage to 8/10 patterns proven composable. Two to go (`kv_write`, `tiled_matmul`).

- **gemv-then-elementwise-double**: `fused_gemv_dequant тЖТ elementwise-double`. GEMV emits per-PE partials, elementwise doubles, sum_across_pe reconstructs `2 ├Ч gemv_result`. End-to-end err = 6.1e-05 (bit_close). Adds `fused_gemv_dequant` to proven patterns.
- **attention-tiled-then-sample**: `attention_tiled тЖТ sample`. Attention output (head_dim=32 per PE) fed as logits into a chunk_size=32 recompile of sample; each PE emits its local_max_val. End-to-end err = 1.19e-07 (bit_close). Adds `sample` to proven patterns.

**New chain-driver primitive:** `load_expected` reference kind тАФ seed generator pre-computes the expected final tensor and saves it under `params.path`; the chain driver just loads it. Sidesteps re-encoding complex math (Q4K dequant+GEMV) in the reference helper.

**E2B + 31B chainCoverage = 8/10:**

- **Proven (8):** `attention_decode, attention_tiled, element_wise, fused_gemv_dequant, gather, reduction, rope, sample`
- **Unproven (2):** `kv_write, tiled_matmul`

**Chain-parity evidence ladder (now 9 artifacts):**

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| elementwise ├Ч 2 (single) | 2 | 0 | bit_exact |
| elementwise ├Ч 2 (subprocess) | 2 | 0 | bit_exact |
| gather тЖТ elementwise | 2 | 0 | bit_exact |
| rope тЖТ attention_tiled | 2 | 1.49e-07 | bit_close |
| gather тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled | 3 | 1.19e-07 | bit_close |
| reduce тЖТ elementwise-double | 2 | 5.72e-06 | bit_close |

**Gates green (7/7):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK detected), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (E2B + 31B chainCoverage >= 8), kernel-chain-parity ├Ч 2 (both new chains bit_close), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: Chain-parity coverage 4/10 тЖТ 6/10 (reduction + attention_decode) (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** two new chains, both bit-close end-to-end, lifting E2B + 31B chainCoverage to 6/10 distinct host-plan kernel patterns proven composable.

- **reduce-then-double**: `reduce_sum_workgroup тЖТ elementwise-double`. Each PE sums its first 256 input elements to output[pe_id] (the workgroup-internal reduction), then elementwise doubles the whole buffer; post-chain sum_across_pe assembles the per-PE reductions into a single vector. End-to-end err = 5.72e-06 (bit_close), adds `reduction` to proven patterns. New reference kind `reduce_then_double` in `bench/tools/run_kernel_chain.py`.
- **rope-then-attention-decode**: `rope тЖТ attention_decode`. Decode-phase variant of the earlier ropeтЖТattention_tiled chain тАФ same rope step, but attention_decode runs at q_len=1 (single-query) rather than q_len=32. End-to-end err = 1.49e-07 (bit_close), adds `attention_decode` to proven patterns.

## Push: 3-kernel Gemma-prefill chain тАФ gather тЖТ rope тЖТ attention bit-close (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the first 3-kernel Gemma-prefill thread. Chain driver gains `postStepTransform` so kernels whose per-PE semantics require an intermediate reduce/broadcast can compose cleanly.

- **gather тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled** (4 PE, hidden_size=head_dim=32, num_tokens=1, num_pairs=16, kv_len=64)
- Step 0 gather: embed lookup; per-PE partials
- Step 0 post-step transform: `sum_and_broadcast` reduces per-PE partials across PEs and broadcasts the full embed back to every PE so step 1 sees real Q
- Step 1 rope: rotates Q in place via per-PE cos/sin tables
- Step 2 attention-tiled: flash attention on rotated Q + per-PE K/V
- **End-to-end max_abs_err = 1.19e-07**, laneStatus = `bit_close`
- Sample expected vs actual match to 8 decimal places:

  ```
  expected: [-0.25351521, -0.17316425, -0.08224778, -0.26269796]
  actual:   [-0.25351527, -0.17316425, -0.08224781, -0.26269796]
  ```

- Receipt at `bench/out/kernel-chain-evidence/gather-rope-attention/chain-parity.json`
- New reference kind `gather_rope_attention` composes `flash_attention(rope(table[index]), K, V)` against numpy
- Gather recompiled at `hidden_size=32, num_tokens=1` to match rope/attention head_dim

**New chain-driver primitive тАФ `postStepTransform`:** each step's output can carry a transform that mutates the `.npy` on disk before the next step reads. Today's kinds: `sum_across_pe` / `broadcast_to_pe` / `sum_and_broadcast`. Composes with the existing per-tensor `chunkSize` and `finalReduce` machinery.

**Chain-parity evidence ladder (now 4 artifacts):**

| chain | kernels | err | status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| elementwise ├Ч 2 (single) | 2, same | 0.0 | bit_exact |
| elementwise ├Ч 2 (subprocess) | 2, same | 0.0 | bit_exact |
| gather тЖТ elementwise | 2, mixed | 0.0 | bit_exact |
| rope тЖТ attention_tiled | 2, Gemma | 1.49e-07 | bit_close |
| **gather тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled** | **3, Gemma** | **1.19e-07** | **bit_close** |

**Gates green (7/7):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK detected), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (E2B + 31B structural_full_coverage), kernel-chain-parity (gatherтЖТropeтЖТattn bit_close), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: First Gemma-prefill slice chain тАФ rope тЖТ attention_tiled bit-close (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the first model-shaped kernel chain. Two non-trivial Gemma kernels composed end-to-end with bit-close numerical parity against a numpy reference that implements the same math.

- **rope тЖТ attention_tiled** (4 PE, head_dim=32, num_pairs=16, kv_len=64, q_len=32)
- Step 1 rotates Q in place via per-PE cos/sin tables
- Step 2 consumes rotated Q + K/V from host and emits attention output
- **End-to-end max_abs_err = 1.49e-07**, laneStatus = `bit_close`
- Sample expected vs actual match to 7+ decimal places:

  ```
  expected: [0.24027469, 0.09429707, 0.14353740, -0.05973017]
  actual:   [0.24027474, 0.09429708, 0.14353737, -0.05973016]
  ```

- Receipt at `bench/out/kernel-chain-evidence/rope-then-attention/chain-parity.json`
- New reference kind `rope_then_attention` in `bench/tools/run_kernel_chain.py` composing both math ops
- Rope recompiled at head_dim=32 (default was 128) to match attention-tiled's shape
- Per-tensor chunk_size on every input/output (rope Q=32, cos/sin=16, attention Q/O=32, K/V=2048) тАФ adapter schema lets kernels with heterogeneous per-PE shapes be chained cleanly

**Why it matters:** this is the first artifact that shows two distinct Doe-emitted Gemma kernels composing with measurable numerical parity, not just two trivial elementwise ops or a gather+scalar combo. RoPE applied to Q, then softmax(QK^T)┬╖V, all driven by real SDK runtime. Extending to a 3тАУ4-kernel chain (gather тЖТ rmsnorm тЖТ q_proj тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled) is now a shape-plumbing exercise rather than a new architecture.

**Gates green (7/7):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK detected), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (E2B + 31B structural_full_coverage), kernel-chain-parity (ropeтЖТattention bit_close), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: Mixed-kernel chain parity тАФ gather тЖТ elementwise bit-exact (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** unblocked user item #4's different-kernel composition. Subprocess-boundary chain driver + first mixed-kernel chain (gather тЖТ elementwise-double) end-to-end bit-exact against numpy.

**Infrastructure:**

- `bench/runners/csl-runners/chain_step_adapter.py` тАФ generic single-step kernel adapter: reads `.npy` input tensors, memcpy_h2d's them to named device symbols with per-tensor chunk_size + dtype, launches compute, memcpy_d2h's outputs to `.npy`. Each spawn is its own SDK lifecycle.
- `bench/tools/run_kernel_chain.py` тАФ chain-spec-driven orchestrator. Spawns `cs_python chain_step_adapter.py` per step. Subprocess boundaries reset SDK global state, dodging the `simfab_api.cc:111: Assertion '0' failed` that multiple in-process SdkRuntime instances trigger. Supports optional `finalReduce: sum_across_pe` for gather-style kernels where the host reconstructs the whole via per-PE partials.
- Chain payloads are 32-bit f32/u32 today (spec'd in the adapter docs as a known limitation for pre-streaming-runtime).

**Evidence:**

| chain | steps | kinds | end-to-end err | laneStatus |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| elementwise-double-x2 | 2 | same-kernel single-runtime | 0.0 | bit_exact (prior iteration) |
| elementwise-double-x2-subprocess | 2 | same-kernel via subprocess | 0.0 | **bit_exact** (proves subprocess boundary) |
| gather-then-elementwise-double | 2 | **mixed-kernel via subprocess** | 0.0 | **bit_exact** |

The gather тЖТ elementwise chain is the first artifact that composes two distinct Doe-emitted CSL kernels end-to-end. Numpy reference: `(table[indices] * 2.0).ravel()` matches post-reduce device output bit-for-bit; sample expected/actual identical.

**Three chain parity receipts under schema-targets + gate (`--require-bit-exact` all three).** Foundation ready for Gemma-prefill slice chains (gather тЖТ rmsnorm тЖТ tiled_matmul тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled тЖТ ...) тАФ the next real model-level parity target.

**Gates green (7/7):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK detected), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (E2B + 31B structural_full_coverage), kernel-chain-parity (bit_exact gatherтЖТdouble), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: Kernel-chain parity harness тАФ bit-exact 2-step composition (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** user-review item #4 foundation тАФ replacing per-kernel parity with multi-kernel end-to-end parity. The first harness runs the simplest meaningful composition.

- `config/doe-kernel-chain-parity.schema.json` тАФ chain receipt shape with steps[] (each step's per-step parity) + endToEndParity + laneStatus (bit_exact / bit_close / structural_only / failed).
- `bench/runners/csl-runners/elementwise_chain_sim_runner.py` тАФ drives a same-kernel 2-step chain (elementwise-double ├Ч 2) via a single SdkRuntime with two sequential compute launches. h2d(input) тЖТ launch тЖТ d2h(output1) тЖТ h2d(output1 as input) тЖТ launch тЖТ d2h(output2). Verifies end-to-end output against `input * 4.0` numpy reference.
- **Result: bit-exact.** step1 err = 0, step2 err = 0, end-to-end err = 0, laneStatus = `bit_exact`. Receipt at `bench/out/kernel-chain-evidence/elementwise-double-x2/chain-parity.json`.
- `bench/gates/kernel_chain_parity_gate.py` тАФ validates receipt + `--require-bit-exact` / `--require-bit-close`.

**SDK constraint surfaced + documented:** two SdkRuntime instances in a single Python process trigger `simfab_api.cc:111: Assertion '0' failed`. This forces same-kernel chains (this harness's shape) to use a single-runtime temporal composition. Different-kernel chains (e.g. gather тЖТ rmsnorm тЖТ tiled_matmul тЖТ rope тЖТ attention_tiled) require either (a) subprocess spawning per kernel with host-file tensor handoff, or (b) PE grid partitioning so each kernel lives on its own rectangle and a single SdkRuntime drives the fabric. Option (b) aligns with the stream-graph's `codeRegions` schema тАФ the future SdkLayout streaming executor is where the different-kernel chain properly lives.

**Why this matters:** this is the first artifact that answers "does Doe compose two kernels end-to-end", not just "does each kernel match numpy in isolation". The user-review item #4 scope is now open тАФ next moves: extend to different-kernel chains (requires one of the options above), then to a Gemma-prefill slice (gather тЖТ rmsnorm тЖТ q_proj тЖТ rope), and eventually to logit-checkpoint parity through the full E2B chain.

**Gates green (7/7):** schema, csl-runtime-fixture (12), wgsl-backend-matrix (12/12, SDK detected), model-receipt ├Ч 2 (E2B + 31B structural_full_coverage), kernel-chain-parity (bit_exact), cmaddr-propagation.

## Push: 31B full-grid compile PROVEN via 2D layout (2026-04-19 UTC)

**Landed:** the 2D layout theory from the prior probe aggregate verified empirically at 31B scale.

- **246├Ч236 = 58,056 PE: PASS (1351.85 s, 22.5 min)** using `bench/out/cslc-grid-probe/elementwise-double-2d/` тАФ a 2D variant of the minimal elementwise kernel with `param width: u16; param height: u16;` and `@set_rectangle(width, height)`. cslc produced **58,056 ELF artifacts (~25 KB each)** under `bench/out/cslc-grid-probe/2d-compile-outputs/246x236/bin/`.
- Matches the preferred unblock path documented last turn in `bench/out/cslc-grid-probe/grid-probe-aggregate.json`. No SDK changes required, no PE partitioning required тАФ just 2D layout emission.
- Compile time scaling: 17,433-PE E2B at 414-440 s, 58,056-PE 31B at 1,352 s. 3.3├Ч PE count тЖТ 3.1├Ч wall time. Super-linear but well within feasibility for one-time compile (especially once the per-layer compile-artifact cache from `doe_stream_graph.compileArtifactCache` lands and all 61 transformer layers share a single ELF).
- Model receipt `fullGridCompileProbeEvidence` now carries `maxProvenPeCount2D: 58056`, `thirtyOneBFullGridCompileVerified: true`, `thirtyOneBCompileSeconds2D: 1351.85`. Both E2B and 31B receipts regenerate cleanly and pass `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-structural-full-coverage --require-fits --min-kernel-coverage-pct 100`.

**executionBlocker ladder state** (per-model): E2B structural+compile proven, 31B structural+compile proven, both gated on `sdk_layout_streaming_executor_missing` (priority #6) for actual execution. Hardware endpoint is the axis after that.

**Remaining work** to flip 31B from `full_grid_compile_unattempted` to `hardware_endpoint_unavailable` in the emitted receipts: propagate the 2D-layout shape (u16 grid params, 2D rectangle) through `runtime/zig/src/doe_wgsl/emit_csl_layout.zig` so every kernel bundle gets the same treatment by default. Then the 17-kernel per-pattern 2D compile sweep becomes tractable.

## Push: 2D layout probe + stream-execution-plan emitter (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:**

- **2D layout probe** (`bench/tools/probe_cslc_2d_grid.py`): tests cslc across `WxH` grids. Added `bench/out/cslc-grid-probe/elementwise-double-2d/` тАФ a 2D variant of the minimal elementwise kernel. Ran 4x2 (8 PE, 6.7s PASS) тЖТ 149x117 (17,433 PE, 414.6s PASS, E2B grid). 246x236 (31B grid, 58,056 PE) probe is still running at this commit тАФ follow-up will record its result.
- **Stream-execution-plan emitter** (`bench/tools/validate_stream_graph.py`): reads a `doe_stream_graph` artifact, runs the schema-declared validations (layerRange non-empty, prefetch lookahead in [1,4], kv policy present, optional real-hash check), and emits a concrete per-layer firing sequence as a `doe_stream_execution_plan` artifact. Schema at `config/doe-stream-execution-plan.schema.json`.
- Both E2B and 31B lanes now emit a stream-execution-plan as the final step. E2B: 35 layers, 2,191 bytes/PE/layer steady-state. 31B: 61 layers, 7,249 bytes/PE/layer steady-state.
- This plan artifact is the shovel-ready hand-off to the future SdkLayout streaming executor (priority #6). `executorStatus: plan_only` until the actual runtime implementation lands.

**Why a 2D probe at all:** last turn's 1D probe surfaced that 31B (58,056 PE flattened) overflows the SDK memcpy module's internal i16 `.width` parameter. 2D layouts keep each axis under i16 max (246x236 тЖТ each dim <= 32,767). 4x2 and 149x117 both pass with the new 2D layout + `u16` grid params, validating the preferred unblock path from the earlier aggregate. 246x236 pending.

**Gates green (6/6):** `schema_gate` (with stream-execution-plan schema), `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (12 fixtures), `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 12 --sdk-optional`, `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-structural-full-coverage` for E2B and 31B, `verify_cmaddr_propagation`.

## Push: cslc grid-limit probe тАФ E2B full-grid compile proven (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** user-review item #3 тАФ "prove full-grid compile" тАФ exercised. `bench/tools/probe_cslc_grid_limits.py` runs cslc on the elementwise-double kernel across 1D grid widths from 4 to 58,056 PEs (31B scale). Produces `bench/out/cslc-grid-probe/grid-probe-aggregate.json`.

**Results:**

| width (peCount) | status | elapsed |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 4 | succeeded | 6.1 s |
| 16 | succeeded | 6.3 s |
| 64 | succeeded | 7.6 s |
| 256 | succeeded | 12.2 s |
| 1,024 | succeeded | 31.7 s |
| 4,096 | succeeded | 107.3 s |
| **17,433 (gemma-4-e2b)** | **succeeded** | **439.7 s** |
| 58,056 (gemma-4-31b) | blocked | 5.6 s |

**E2B compile is real.** The 149├Ч117 grid compiles cleanly in 7.3 minutes wall time for the simplest kernel. cslc linear-log scaling holds well across four orders of magnitude.

**31B blocker, isolated:** the Cerebras SDK's `<memcpy/get_params>` module declares `.width` as i16 internally. 58,056 overflows i16 (max 32,767). The error originates in the SDK module, not in Doe's emitter тАФ fixing Doe's own `param width: i16` to `u16` (in-tree change applied to elementwise-double) is necessary but not sufficient. Three unblock paths documented in the aggregate; **preferred path: emit 2D layouts** (`@set_rectangle(width, height)` where each axis stays under i16 max). 31B's 246├Ч236 fits per-axis without needing SDK changes or PE partitioning.

**Model receipt now carries the probe evidence:** `fullGridCompileProbeEvidence.maxProvenPeCount1D = 17433` and `thirtyOneBRequires2DEmitter = true` are surfaced in every regenerated E2B and 31B receipt.

**Gates green (6/6):** `schema_gate`, `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (12), `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 12 --sdk-optional` (SDK detected), `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-structural-full-coverage` for E2B and 31B, `verify_cmaddr_propagation`.

## Push: Receipt taxonomy + reduceStrategy cleanup (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** taxonomy cleanup so the model-level receipt stops reading as "model executed" when it's only structural coverage, and the partial/fabric reduce tradeoff is now explicit per kernel.

**Receipt taxonomy (user-requested):**

- `laneStatus` renamed to `structural_full_coverage` / `structural_partial_coverage_kernel_gap` / `structural_memory_plan_does_not_fit` (legacy values kept so older receipts parse).
- New `executionStatus` enum: `not_attempted` / `simulator_success` / `simulator_failure` / `hardware_success` / `hardware_failure` / `compile_failure`.
- New `executionBlocker` enum with priority: `partial_kernel_coverage` тЖТ `memory_plan_does_not_fit` тЖТ `sdk_layout_streaming_executor_missing` тЖТ `full_grid_compile_unattempted` тЖТ `hardware_endpoint_unavailable` тЖТ `none`.
- Receipt builder sets `executionStatus=not_attempted` + the first unmet blocker.
- Gate gains `--require-structural-full-coverage` + `--require-execution` flags.
- Both E2B and 31B receipts now honestly read: `laneStatus=structural_full_coverage`, `executionStatus=not_attempted`, `executionBlocker=sdk_layout_streaming_executor_missing`.

**reduceStrategy field:**

- New `reduceStrategy` enum on every fixture in `config/csl-runtime-fixtures.schema.json`: `none`, legacy `on_device_fabric`, `on_device_fabric_validated`, `on_device_fabric_quarantined`, legacy `host_partial`, and canonical `host_reduce_partial`.
- Populated for all 12 fixtures:
  - `on_device_fabric`: `tiled-matmul` (c2d_params broadcast chain on WSE).
  - `host_reduce_partial`: `fused-gemv-dequant`, `sample` (fabric allreduce deferred or intentionally host-combined; partials exported to host with `reduceStrategyNote` carried into model receipts).
  - `none`: remaining 9 kernels (per-PE-only or workgroup-internal reductions).
- Field threaded through `build_model_runtime_receipt.py` so every host-plan kernel in the E2B / 31B receipts carries `reduceStrategy` and optional `reduceStrategyNote`. Downstream tooling (and the future streaming executor) can now tell apart a kernel that needs a host-side reduction step from one whose per-PE output is already the final value.

**Gates green** (6/6): `schema_gate`, `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (12 fixtures), `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 12 --sdk-optional` (SDK detected), `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-structural-full-coverage` for E2B and 31B, `verify_cmaddr_propagation`.

**Remaining work** (unchanged in shape): SdkLayout streaming executor (the actual runtime implementation), full-grid cslc compile receipts for 149├Ч117 / 246├Ч236 layouts, and model-level parity тАФ logit-checkpoint comparison through the graph, not just per-kernel parity against numpy.

## Push: Stream-graph emitter + cmaddr propagation smoke (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** the stream-graph and hardware-endpoint plumbing pieces that sit between the memory plan and the not-yet-built SdkLayout streaming runtime.

- `bench/tools/build_stream_graph.py` тАФ derives a `doe_stream_graph` artifact from the memory plan + model config. Replaces the hardcoded 31B sample with a real emitter that reads `streamStages` and maps stage kind тЖТ (source, muxPattern) via a small table: `embedding_rows тЖТ host_embeddings / broadcast`, `layer_weights тЖТ host_weights / row_broadcast`, `ple_rows / ple_projection тЖТ host_ple_table / column_broadcast`, `kv_stream тЖТ kv_overflow / unicast`. Ring-buffer depth defaults to 2 (double-buffered prefetch).
- Lane drivers (`bench/runners/run_e2b_full_graph_lane.py`, `bench/runners/run_31b_full_graph_lane.py`) now emit the stream-graph as the final pipeline step alongside the model-level receipt.
- Generated: `bench/out/e2b-full-graph/gemma-4-e2b-stream-graph.json` (4 streams, 35-layer code region) and `bench/out/31b-full-graph/gemma-4-31b-stream-graph.json` (4 streams, 61-layer code region). Both validate under `schema_gate`.
- `bench/tools/verify_cmaddr_propagation.py` тАФ priority #7 hardware-endpoint plumbing verifier. Unit-tests the driver's pure functions (`materialize_command` + `redact_command_for_receipt` + execution-target classification) with simfabric (empty cmaddr) and system (fake cmaddr) cases. Runs in milliseconds without invoking `cslc` or `cs_python` or needing a real endpoint. Asserts: empty cmaddr drops the `{cmaddr_arg}` slot cleanly; non-empty cmaddr embeds `--cmaddr=IP:PORT`; the recorded receipt replaces the raw endpoint with `$DOE_CSL_CMADDR`; `executionTarget` flips `simfabric` тЖФ `system` on cmaddr presence. Proves the hardware-endpoint path is wired end-to-end without requiring a live CS system, so the E2B-on-hardware step can land the moment an endpoint becomes available.

**Gates green:** `schema_gate`, `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (12 fixtures), `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 12 --sdk-optional` (SDK detected), `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-fits --require-full-coverage --min-kernel-coverage-pct 100` for both E2B and 31B.

**Next:** the actual SdkLayout streaming-runtime implementation remains the big follow-up тАФ async DSDs for prefetch, ring-buffer management, compile-artifact cache lookup, KV spill-to-host. The stream-graph schema lets this implementation work land in stages without blocking downstream consumers.

## Push: Gemma 4 31B lane + streaming-migration receipt + stream-graph schema (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** priorities #5 (31B memory-plan migration) and #6 (SdkLayout streaming-runtime schema skeleton). Evidence that Doe's existing plan-chain scales from E2B to 31B structurally and that the runtime-path boundary between memcpy RPC and streaming runtime is explicit.

**31B lane:**

- `runtime/zig/examples/execution-v1/gemma-4-31b-smoke.json` тАФ scaled from E2B (hidden=5120, heads=32, layers=61, same step graph, same vocab/PLE shape)
- `bench/runners/run_31b_full_graph_lane.py` тАФ end-to-end driver
- `bench/out/31b-full-graph/` тАФ host-plan, memory-plan, runtime-config, simulator-plan, runtime receipt
- Result: 246├Ч236 = **58,056 PEs, 34.2 GB total model, fits=true, 17/17 kernel coverage, full_coverage lane status**
- Compile-artifact reuse factor: 61 тАФ all transformer layers share one compile shape

**Streaming migration derivation** (both E2B and 31B receipts now carry):

- `perPeSramBudget`, `headroomBytesPerPe` (E2B: 8 bytes, 31B: 4 bytes тАФ razor-thin by current planner)
- `maxPerLayerStage` vs `maxSetupStage` тАФ distinguishes per-layer streaming workload (repeatCount > 1, double-buffered) from one-shot init stages
- `doubleBufferedWorkingSetPerPe` + `doubleBufferedFits` (both models: fits=true for per-layer double-buffering)
- `compileArtifactReuseFactor` (E2B: 35├Ч, 31B: 61├Ч) тАФ direct measure of the per-layer compile cache savings
- `runtimePath` тИИ {`memcpy_rpc`, `sdk_layout_streaming`} with `streamingRuntimeRequired` boolean тАФ both E2B and 31B flag streaming runtime required because `streamed_working_set_per_pe > per_pe_sram / 2` (embeddings dominate SRAM)

**Stream-graph schema** (`config/doe-stream-graph.schema.json`):

Captures the SdkLayout streaming-runtime config knobs before the runtime itself is implemented:

- `codeRegions` тАФ per-layer ELF placement (compile-artifact sha256 + PE range + layer range). Different layers sharing compile shape reuse one region.
- `streams` тАФ async prefetch streams with source (host_weights / host_embeddings / host_ple_table / kv_overflow / activation_input), destinationPort, ringBufferDepth, payloadBytes, muxPattern (broadcast / row_broadcast / column_broadcast / unicast / demux_round_robin).
- `prefetchSchedule` тАФ lookaheadLayers (1-4), kickoffTrigger (layer_start / activation_ready / unblock_signal), stallPolicy (fail_closed / backpressure / drop_oldest).
- `kvPolicy` тАФ residency (resident / spill_to_host / partitioned_across_pes), spillBehavior (eager / on_demand / lru), maxResidentTokens.
- `compileArtifactCache` тАФ key/value SHA-256 hash lookup; per_session vs shared_across_sessions.
- `validation` тАФ fail-closed routing reachability + port binding + acyclicity booleans.

Sample 31B stream-graph at `bench/out/31b-full-graph/gemma-4-31b-stream-graph.json` validates under `schema_gate`. The implementation of the actual runtime (code regions + async DSDs + ring buffer + compile-artifact cache lookup) is the next follow-up.

**Gates green:** `schema_gate` (with new stream-graph + receipt schemas), `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-fits --require-full-coverage --min-kernel-coverage-pct 100` passes for **both E2B and 31B**.

## Push: E2B full coverage тАФ sample + kv_write runtime-ready, 12/12 matrix (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** the two remaining E2B kernel-pattern gaps closed тАФ gemma-4-e2b-it-text-q4k-ehf16-af32 now flips from `partial_coverage_kernel_gap` (14/17 = 82%) to **`full_coverage` (17/17 = 100%)**.

- **sample** runtime-ready: variant pe_program exports per-PE `(local_max_val, local_max_idx)`; host computes global argmax. For 4096-vocab ├Ч 4 PE, selects token **1913 bit-for-bit** identical to numpy argmax. Same host-side-reduce pattern as fused_gemv_dequant тАФ bypasses the async-send fabric-reduce teardown stall.
- **kv_write** runtime-ready: standalone variant with fixed-size local `k_cache`/`v_cache` buffers per PE. Writes the K/V projections at `position=7` and the runner verifies `write_err=0.0`, `stray_abs=0.0` (no spillage into neighboring slots). Surfaced + fixed a latent emitter bug: `@as(u32, @intCast(head_dim))` in `emit_csl_kv_cache.zig` тАФ `@intCast` is not a CSL builtin, replaced with `@as(u32, head_dim)`.
- Schema fix: `config/csl-runtime-fixtures.schema.json` kernelPattern enum extended with `kv_write`.

**Matrix after push:** 12 rows, Vulkan SPIR-V 12/12, Metal MSL 12/12, D3D12 HLSL+DXIL 12/12, **CSL runtime 12/12**. All Gemma HostPlan kernel-pattern outcomes relevant to 270M/E2B are runtime-parity-verified on the Cerebras WSE-3 simulator.

**E2B receipt:** `bench/gates/model_runtime_receipt_gate.py --require-fits --require-full-coverage --min-kernel-coverage-pct 100` passes. 149├Ч117 grid (17,433 PEs), residencyMode=layer_streaming, fits=true.

**Next under the plan roadmap:** priority #5 31B memory-plan migration (layer_streaming residency + streamed weight shards + per-layer compile-artifact reuse cache) and #6 SdkLayout streaming runtime (code regions, ports, streams, async send/receive, demux/mux). These are schema-expansion + new-runtime-path work beyond the current resident E2B shape.

## Push: Gemma 4 E2B full-graph lane + model-level runtime receipt (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** priorities #3 and #4 from the CSL plan roadmap тАФ an end-to-end E2B lane driver that converts the model config manifest into HostPlan + memory-plan + runtime-config + simulator-plan, plus a model-level runtime receipt that binds every artifact by SHA-256 and resolves each host-plan kernel to its CSL runtime-ready fixture.

**E2B evidence (gemma-4-e2b-it-text-q4k-ehf16-af32):**

- Grid: 149 ├Ч 117 = **17,433 PEs**
- Residency mode: **layer_streaming** (E2B already uses streaming, not resident)
- Memory: 6.88 GB total (51.4 MB persistent + 6.84 GB streamed), 99% SRAM utilization, **fits = true**
- 17 kernels classified; 14 runtime-ready (82% coverage); 3 missing: `kv_write` (├Ч2) + `sample`
- 20 prefill launches + 23 decode launches

**New artifacts:**

- `bench/runners/run_e2b_full_graph_lane.py` тАФ single-command driver for the whole pipeline
- `bench/tools/build_model_runtime_receipt.py` тАФ binds manifest + host-plan + memory-plan + runtime-config + simulator-plan + fixture registry into a model-level receipt; id-first fixture lookup with pattern fallback (so gelu resolves to the gelu fixture rather than the first element_wise fixture)
- `config/doe-model-runtime-receipt.schema.json` тАФ schema registered in `config/schema-targets.json`
- `bench/gates/model_runtime_receipt_gate.py` тАФ validates the receipt with `--require-fits`, `--require-full-coverage`, and `--min-kernel-coverage-pct N` flags
- `bench/out/e2b-full-graph/gemma-4-e2b-runtime-receipt.{json,md}` тАФ first published receipt

**Gates green:** `model_runtime_receipt_gate --require-fits --min-kernel-coverage-pct 80` passes for E2B (coverage=14/17 = 82%, fits=True). `schema_gate` passes with the new receipt in the schema-targets registry.

**Why this matters:** this is the first artifact that answers "can Doe run this model end-to-end" at the model level rather than the kernel level. It's also the structural template 31B will extend with a streaming-runtime path тАФ the `residencyMode=layer_streaming` field and `streamStages` in the memory plan are already where 31B's extra metadata will live (stream buffer sizing, per-layer compile-artifact reuse cache, KV-cache residency policy).

**Next:** close the 3-kernel gap (kv_write + sample) to flip E2B's laneStatus from `partial_coverage_kernel_gap` тЖТ `full_coverage`. Then 31B memory-plan migration (priority #5) and SdkLayout streaming runtime (priority #6).

## Push: CSL runtime coverage to 10 тАФ fused_gemv_dequant via host-reduce variant (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** fused_gemv_dequant promoted to the 10th CSL runtime-ready fixture, completing the Gemma kernel-pattern coverage relevant to 270M/E2B.

- **Kernel:** Q4K dequant (f16 scale + 128 packed nibble-bytes per 144-byte block) fused with per-PE GEMV. Each PE dequants its weight slice and computes `partial[out_dim]` via scalar dot products; the host memcpy_d2h's per-PE partials and sums across PEs. Verified bit-close against a numpy Q4K dequant+GEMV reference on 4 PE ├Ч out_dim=64 ├Ч in_dim_per_pe=512: `per_pe_err=4.2e-05`, `reduce_err=4.2e-05`.
- **Fabric allreduce deferred**: the primary emitted `pe_program.csl` (`bench/out/dual-compile-evidence/fused-gemv-dequant/csl/pe_program.csl`) uses a hand-rolled async-send chain that has a known teardown-ordering stall (documented in iter-35/36 of the original runtime-run/result.json). Adopting the canonical `<collectives_2d>` or `<benchmark-libs/allreduce>` module is a multi-day rewrite. This fixture uses a `runtime/zig/examples/simulator/fused-gemv-dequant-runtime/compile/fused-gemv-dequant/pe_program.csl` variant that exports `partial` and does host-side reduction. Proves dequant + per-PE GEMV correctness today; fabric-reduce adoption is tracked separately in the governed-lane-report's `variantNotes.fabricReduce`.

**Matrix after push:** 10 rows, Vulkan SPIR-V 10/10, Metal MSL 10/10, D3D12 HLSL+DXIL 10/10, **CSL runtime 10/10**. All Gemma HostPlan kernel-pattern outcomes relevant to 270M/E2B are now runtime-parity-verified on the Cerebras WSE-3 simulator.

**Gates green:** `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (10 fixtures), `schema_gate`, `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 10 --sdk-optional --require-vulkan/metal/d3d12-ready` (SDK detected, threshold enforced).

**Next under user's priority list (post-kernel coverage):** priority #3 E2B full-graph lane (WGSL kernels тЖТ classifier тЖТ HostPlan тЖТ memory plan тЖТ CSL bundles тЖТ operationGraph тЖТ runtime-config тЖТ simulator trace), then #4 model-level runtime receipt binding model/tokenizer config hash + HostPlan hash + memory-plan hash + backend artifact hashes + numerical parity.

## Push: CSL runtime coverage to 9 тАФ attention_tiled + attention_decode + matrix gate (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** two Gemma attention kernels promoted to CSL runtime-ready, and the cross-backend matrix gate wired into the blocking bundle with SDK-optional CSL.

- **attention_tiled** (prefill Flash Attention): max_abs_err=2.24e-07 on 4 PE ├Ч head_dim=32 ├Ч kv_len=64 ├Ч q_len=32. The tiled_matmul DSD .offset fix did NOT apply here тАФ attention_tiled uses scalar-indexed array loops (no @get_dsd calls), not @fmacs DSD flow. Fixture at `runtime/zig/examples/simulator/attention-tiled-runtime/`, runner at `bench/runners/csl-runners/attention_tiled_sim_runner.py` (shares `common.py`).
- **attention_decode** (single-query decode): max_abs_err=1.79e-07 on 4 PE ├Ч head_dim=32 ├Ч kv_len=64 ├Ч q_len=1. Shares emitter body with attention_tiled; only q_len differs. Fixture at `runtime/zig/examples/simulator/attention-decode-runtime/`.
- **Matrix lock:** `bench/gates/wgsl_backend_matrix_gate.py` now supports `--sdk-optional` with a `csl_sdk_detected()` helper that checks DOE_CSL_SDK_ROOT, DOE_CSLC_EXECUTABLE, and `cslc` on PATH. When SDK is present, `--min-csl-runtime-ready N` is enforced; when absent, the threshold is informational. Wired into `bench/runners/run_blocking_gates.py` via `--with-wgsl-backend-matrix-gate` + `--wgsl-backend-matrix-min-csl-runtime-ready N`. This is user priority #1 тАФ prevents regressions across the shared WGSL emitter path as more Gemma kernels land, without gating on hosts that don't have the Cerebras SDK installed.

**Matrix after push:** 9 rows, Vulkan SPIR-V 9/9, Metal MSL 9/9, D3D12 HLSL+DXIL 9/9, **CSL runtime 9/9**. All Gemma HostPlan kernel-pattern outcomes relevant to 270M/E2B are now both compile-green and runtime-parity-verified on the Cerebras WSE-3 simulator.

**Gates green:** `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (9 fixtures), `schema_gate`, `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 9 --sdk-optional --require-vulkan/metal/d3d12-ready`, `csl_fixture_mirror_gate`, `csl_operation_graph_gate`.

**Next under user's priority list:** fused_gemv_dequant runtime (still has async-send stall in a different code path), then E2B full-graph lane, then model-level runtime receipt, then 31B memory-plan migration + SdkLayout streaming runtime.

## Push: CSL tiled_matmul bit-exact runtime parity + registry row (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Landed:** iteration 43 closed out the SUMMA tiled_matmul kernel to **bit-exact numerical parity** (max_abs_err=0.0) on the Cerebras SDK 1.4 simulator for 16x16 @ 16x16 on a 2x2 PE grid, and registered it as the 6th runtime-ready CSL fixture.

**Root cause (emitter-side, not host-side):** Doe's `emit_csl_matmul.zig` was positioning A_dsd per-k via `.offset = k*Mt` inside `@get_dsd(mem1d_dsd, .{ .base_address = Ap, .extent = Mt, .offset = ... })`. No canonical SDK example uses that field in the constructor; the value was silently mis-interpreted. The canonical SUMMA pattern (`csl-extras/examples/benchmarks/gemm-collectives_2d/pe.csl`) declares A_dsd outside the k-loop via `.tensor_access = |i|{Mt} -> A_tile[i]` + `@set_dsd_base_addr(A_dsd, Ap)` and advances at end of each k via `A_dsd = @increment_dsd_offset(A_dsd, Mt, f32)`. Prior diagnosis wrongly blamed host tile placement (iter-31 row-major gave max_abs_err=15.7; iter-43 canonical col-major gave 16.9 тАФ larger, not smaller, confirming the bug was emitter-side).

**Contract changes:**

- `config/doe-wgsl-simulator-plan.schema.json`: added optional `compileTargets[*].compileParams` object so kernels that declare top-level layout params beyond width/height (tiled_matmul needs P:2,Mt:8,Kt:8,Nt:8) keep the governed plan as the single source of truth.
- `runtime/zig/tools/csl_sdk_driver.py`: honors `compileParams`, appending `key:value` pairs to the cslc `--params` argument.
- `runtime/zig/src/doe_wgsl/emit_csl_simulator.zig`: the Zig sim-runner plan parser now uses `ignore_unknown_fields = true` so the shared schema can carry driver-only metadata (sourceWgslPath, compileParams) without breaking the Zig consumer.

**New fixture artifacts:**

- `runtime/zig/examples/simulator/tiled-matmul-runtime/{host-plan.json, runtime-config.json, simulator-plan.template.json, compile/tiled-matmul/*.csl}`
- `bench/runners/csl-runners/tiled_matmul_sim_runner.py` (uses shared `common.py`)
- `bench/out/dual-compile-evidence/governed-lane-sdk-handoff/sim-success-tiled-matmul/{governed-lane-report.json, driver-result.json, trace.json, host-plan.json}`
- Added entry in `config/csl-runtime-fixtures.json` (now 7 fixtures, 6 runtime_ready).

**Matrix summary** (regenerated `bench/out/cross-backend-matrix/wgsl-backend-matrix.json`): 7 rows, Vulkan SPIR-V 7/7, Metal MSL 7/7, D3D12 HLSL+DXIL 7/7, CSL runtime **7/7** after the parallel GELU bump (tanh approximation, runtimeMaxAbsErr=9.5e-07 on 16 PE ├Ч 1024 f32).

**Gates green:** `csl_runtime_fixture_gate --require-ready-receipts` (7 fixtures), `schema_gate`, `wgsl_backend_matrix_gate --min-csl-runtime-ready 6 --require-vulkan-ready --require-metal-ready --require-d3d12-ready`, `zig build test`, `zig build test-wgsl`.

**Remaining work under user's iter-42 plan #4:** attention_tiled, attention_decode, fused_gemv_dequant need the same runtime-ready bump. attention_tiled likely inherits the same emitter fix (shares the c2d/SUMMA skeleton). fused_gemv_dequant still has an async-send stall in a different code path.

## Push: WGSL backend matrix + CSL runtime fixture registry (2026-04-18 UTC)

Added a first-class registry for governed CSL runtime fixtures:
`config/csl-runtime-fixtures.json` + schema. The registry binds the
runtime-ready CSL fixtures for elementwise, gather, rope, attention-linear, and
reduction, plus the compile-ready GELU fixture, to their WGSL source, HostPlan,
runtime config, runner, governed-lane report, driver result, and trace
artifacts.

Added `bench/gates/csl_runtime_fixture_gate.py` so the registry checks the
referenced simulator plans, HostPlans, runtime commands, runner scripts, and
ready governed-lane reports. The gate supports a stricter
`--require-ready-receipts` mode for SDK-backed environments.

Added HLSL and native DXIL emitter CLIs (`doe-emit-hlsl`, `doe-emit-dxil`) next
to the existing SPIR-V and MSL tools. `bench/tools/build_wgsl_backend_matrix.py`
now builds a matrix keyed by the same WGSL source and can emit MSL/HLSL/DXIL
artifacts while reporting Vulkan SPIR-V and CSL governed-lane evidence. The
generated report schema is `config/wgsl-backend-matrix-report.schema.json`, and
`bench/gates/wgsl_backend_matrix_gate.py` validates the result with optional
per-backend readiness requirements.

The CSL runtime runners now share `bench/runners/csl-runners/common.py` for
argument parsing, endpoint handling, max-error computation, and
`explicit_simulator_trace` writing. This is the first runner-template surface
before promoting tiled matmul, attention tiled/decode, and fused GEMV dequant.

**Changed (7):**

- `runtime/zig/src/dropin/dropin_runtime_config.zig`: `catch |err| { if (err == error.EnvironmentVariableNotFound) return fallback; return fallback; }` тАФ both arms return `fallback`, so the predicate is dead. Collapsed to `catch return fallback;`. 3 lines тЖТ 1.

**Already clean, no change (visited during the hunt):** `runtime/zig/src/main.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/module_runner.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/main_usage.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/command_stream.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/model.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/ort_ep_anchor.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/ort_ep_session_smoke_anchor.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/ort_ep_smoke_anchor.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/ort_incumbent_session_smoke_anchor.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/main_doe_plan_executor.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/main_webgpu_plan_executor.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/main_runtime_compile_report.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/main_emit_hlsl.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/main_host_hotpath_bench.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/replay.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/doe_vulkan_feature_cache.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/doe_shader_translation_cache.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/doe_shader_compilation_info_native.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/pipeline_cache.zig`, `runtime/zig/src/webgpu_backend_lifecycle.zig`.

## Push: CSL simulator hard gate accepts runtime numerical traces (2026-04-18 UTC)

Promoted the first SDK simulator-success receipt into the hard-gate contract.
`config/doe-wgsl-simulator-trace.schema.json` now accepts both the original
`compile_run_smoke_summary` trace and the new `explicit_simulator_trace`
runtime numerical trace shape emitted by the elementwise-double
`cs_python`/`SdkRuntime` fixture. The runtime trace contract requires
`runtimePassed=true`, target execution mode, element counts, max absolute error,
and input/expected/actual samples.

`bench/gates/csl_simulator_gate.py` now treats `explicit_simulator_trace` as a
real runtime receipt and fails if `runtimePassed` is not true. This lets
`--require-ready` validate the new elementwise-double success receipt instead
of only validating compile-smoke traces.

## Push: 7-file review batch, `parseKind` ladder тЖТ KIND_ALIASES table-driven lookup (2026-04-18 UTC)

**Changed (1 of 7):**

- `runtime/zig/src/command/command_kind.zig`: `parseKind` was a 24-branch ladder of `if (matchesAny(kind, &.{тАж})) { return .X; }` statements mapping JSON command-name aliases to the `NormalizedKind` enum. Extracted into a module-level `KIND_ALIASES: [_]KindAliases{ тАж }` comptime table and replaced the body with a single `inline for (KIND_ALIASES) |entry| { if (matchesAny(kind, entry.aliases)) return entry.kind; }`. Same pattern used for `csl_spec.validateOutput` (fire 38) and `hlsl_renamed_builtin` (fire 41). The `inline for` still unrolls at compile-time so the per-alias `commandKindEquals` matches stay comptime-known. Net: ~90 lines of branches тЖТ ~50-line table + 5-line loop. `zig build test` and `zig build test-wgsl` both green.

- `browser/chromium/scripts/check-browser-milestones.py`: `main`'s `if args.emit_json: ... else: ...` pair used 2-space indent on the two `print` / `emit_text(summary)` bodies while the rest of the file uses 4-space PEP 8 style. Restored to 4 spaces. Pure style, no behavior change.
- `runtime/bridge/onnxruntime-ep/src/doe_ort_ep_exports.cc`: the `DOE_ORT_EP_EXPORT` macro definition had three branches тАФ `_WIN32` (uses `__declspec(dllexport)`), `__APPLE__` (uses `__attribute__((visibility("default")))`), and `else` (also uses `__attribute__((visibility("default")))`). The `__APPLE__` and fallback branches were byte-identical, so the `__APPLE__` arm was dead. Collapsed into a two-branch `_WIN32` / else macro. 7 lines тЖТ 5, identical expansion on every platform.

Each `flipObserved` set comprehension appears once (no double-build to hoist); `build_claim`'s `any(...)` generators are used once each. The `[logits[index] - exact_reference_logits[index] for index in range(len(logits))]` comprehension could become `zip`-based, but `zip` silently truncates on length mismatch whereas `range(len(logits))` would raise `IndexError` тАФ kept the indexed form as a defensive guard.

## Push: 7-file review batch, `SemVer.cmp` via `std.math.order` (2026-04-18 UTC)

Eighth 7-files-per-fire batch, all files from the `model_*` family.

**Changed (1 of 7):**

- `runtime/zig/src/model_profile.zig`: `SemVer.cmp` was an open-coded cascade of `if (self.X > other.X) return .gt; if (self.X < other.X) return .lt;` for each of the three semver fields (major/minor/patch). Replaced each pair with `std.math.order(self.X, other.X)` тАФ the stdlib's own comparison helper тАФ and short-circuit return when `.eq` fails. 8 if-statements collapse to a three-step `order` / early-return / `order` chain. All 7 existing `SemVer` tests (parse variants + ordering combinations) pass unchanged.

**Already clean, no change (6 of 7):**

- `runtime/zig/src/model_async_types.zig`: 32 lines тАФ async-diagnostics + map-async enums and structs, pure data.
- `runtime/zig/src/model_commands.zig`: 222-line dispatch facade. The comptime coherence check between `Command` / `CoreCommand` / `FullCommand` has two near-parallel `for (fields)` loops but they're comptime-only (one compile-time run), so DRY has no runtime cost to recover. The `as_core_command` / `as_full_command` switches could be comptime-generated via `inline for` over union fields, but the explicit listing is greppable and matches the CoreCommand/FullCommand partition definition directly.

## Push: optional CSL simulator gate and CM endpoint plumbing (2026-04-18 UTC)

Added the opt-in CSL simulator receipt gate to `run_blocking_gates.py` via
`--with-csl-simulator-gate`. The gate validates the governed CSL report and its
referenced simulator/driver/trace artifacts when present, but only requires
`laneStatus=ready` when `--csl-simulator-require-ready` is set. This keeps
hosts without the Cerebras SDK in the explicit `blocked` diagnostic path instead
of making SDK absence a default blocking failure.

`run_csl_governed_lane.py` now accepts `--csl-sdk-root` and resolves `cslc` /
`cs_python` from that SDK root unless explicit executable flags are supplied.
It also forwards `--csl-cmaddr IP_ADDRESS:PORT` through `$DOE_CSL_CMADDR` so
the SDK runtime command can target a CS system. Driver receipts record
`executionTarget` and `cmaddrProvided`, and persisted command arrays redact the
actual endpoint as `$DOE_CSL_CMADDR`; credentials remain external SDK
environment state.

The runtime-config schema now permits `mode="sdk-runtime-command"` with an
explicit command template, while preserving existing `compile-only` fixtures.
Docs in `docs/process.md`, `docs/csl-architecture.md`, and `bench/README.md`
now describe the optional simulator gate, simfabric default, and CS-system
endpoint handoff.

## Push: `command/command_parse_dispatch.zig` dispatch-dimension parse collapse (2026-04-18 UTC)

Tenth random-file review fire. `runtime/zig/src/command/command_parse_dispatch.zig::parseDispatchDimensions` had three parallel branches picking the dispatch grid source: first `raw.workgroupCount`, then `raw.workgroups`, then per-axis `raw.x` / `raw.y` / `raw.z` with `orelse 1` fallbacks. The first two branches were byte-identical three-line array copies.

Both `workgroupCount` and `workgroups` are typed `?[3]u32` on the raw payload (verified at `runtime/zig/src/command_json_raw.zig:293-294`), so the whole cascade collapses into a single `orelse` chain:

```zig
const dims: [3]u32 = raw.workgroupCount orelse raw.workgroups orelse .{
    raw.x orelse 1,
    raw.y orelse 1,
    raw.z orelse 1,
};
```

22 lines down to 9. Same precedence (workgroupCount > workgroups > x/y/z), same zero-dim rejection, same return shape. Other files scanned this fire (`command/command_kind.zig`, `doe_queue_submit_shared.zig`) were already in DRY form тАФ the `matchesAny` helper dedupes the string-alias handling, and the backend switch in `flush_pending_work_dropin_sync` already uses the same shape as the `doeNativeQueueRelease` cleanup from fire 10.

Validation: `zig build test` тЖТ PASS; `zig build test-wgsl` тЖТ PASS.

## Push: matvec RADV ISA investigation тАФ clamp removal broke MLP (2026-04-18 UTC)

Paired clamped-vs-elided SPIR-V investigation of `compute_matvec_32768x2048_f32_naive_swizzle0`, which regressed p50/p95/p99 by ~11.6% on the 2026-04-18T20:02:10Z AMD Vulkan release claim despite the proof-backed elided SPIR-V having ~15% fewer bytes and 18 fewer scalar ops. Full artifact bundle at `bench/out/matvec-radv-investigation/20260418T212609Z/` with `investigation.json`, `spirv-diff.md`, both SPIR-V binaries + `spirv-dis` output, RADV/ACO dumps from `RADV_DEBUG=shaders` on a Radeon 8060S (STRIX_HALO, Mesa 26.0.3, RDNA 3.5), and the loop-body NIR for each variant.

Finding: the regression is not a proof-pipeline defect. At the ACO level both variants emit **identical** ssbo-load counts (10), identical FMA counts (32), identical `s_waitcnt` counts (6), and identical max-VGPR pressure (v[23]). Scalar pressure drops by 4 registers in the elided form (s[19] тЖТ s[15]), confirming the clamp was real SALU work, not a dead-code no-op.

The NIR loop-body diff reveals the actual cause. In the clamped form, the four matrix-row addresses are computed from four independent pre-staged base registers (`%20`, `%24`, `%26`, `%28`), one per row; the four matrix loads are thus independent in the dataflow and the hardware can issue them as 4-way memory-level parallel requests. In the elided form, NIR's stride-collapse pass proves the four row addresses form a strided `{base, base+0x2000, base+0x4000, base+0x6000}` series and rewrites each row's address as an `iadd` chained from the previous row's address `%29`. Matrix loads now serialize through that chain, and the ~11.6% regression is consistent with losing 4-way MLP on the critical matrix-read path.

The clamp was not dead code at the scheduler level: `umin(base + k, N)` is not commutative with `iadd` when the sum exceeds `N`, so its presence blocked stride-collapse and implicitly preserved MLP. Removing it was correct-by-semantics but traded MLP for instruction count, which on RDNA 3.5 is the wrong trade for this kernel shape. `compute_matvec_32768x2048_f32_swizzle1` and `compute_matvec_32768x2048_f32_workgroupshared_swizzle1` both remain claimable because their matrix access patterns don't rely on independent row addresses for MLP.

Follow-up recommendation: accept the naive regression as an RDNA scheduler artifact rather than reintroduce the clamp or add a stride-collapse fence. The optimized swizzle1 / workgroupshared variants benefit from the same proof chain and claim fine; the naive variant is the uninteresting baseline. Alternative paths (WGSL-level anti-optimization barrier; upstream ACO heuristic; matrix pre-swizzle) are recorded in `investigation.json` as follow-up options but not prioritized.

## Push: `bench_synthetic_assets.zig` slice simplification (2026-04-18 UTC)

Eighth random-file review fire, small surgical change.

`runtime/zig/src/bench_synthetic_assets.zig::readAssetWords` was reading little-endian u32s from a byte buffer via `std.mem.readInt(u32, bytes[byte_index .. byte_index + @sizeOf(u32)][0..@sizeOf(u32)], .little)`. The `[byte_index .. byte_index + @sizeOf(u32)][0..@sizeOf(u32)]` double-slice expresses the same array-pointer type as `[byte_index..][0..@sizeOf(u32)]` but requires computing and sub-slicing the explicit end index. Simplified to the open-ended form; Zig derives the `*const [4]u8` type purely from the second `[0..@sizeOf(u32)]`. Identical bytes read, identical endianness handling, one fewer arithmetic op per loop iteration.

Other files scanned this fire (`doe_label_store.zig`, `runtime/threading_contract.zig`) were already clean тАФ small, focused contract / C-ABI files with nothing to collapse. Survey pass, not every file is a target.

Validation: `zig build test` тЖТ PASS; `zig build test-wgsl` тЖТ PASS.

## Push: `check_core_import_fence.py` import-walk helper + inline-set dedup (2026-04-18 UTC)

Seventh random-file review fire. `runtime/zig/tools/check_core_import_fence.py` had six scan functions, five of which implemented the same nested walk: `for path in sorted(ZIG_SRC.rglob("*.zig")): for line_no, line in enumerate(path.read_text().splitlines(), 1): for match in ZIG_IMPORT_RE.finditer(line): ...`. Every scan reparsed each `.zig` file independently and repeated the candidate-path resolution boilerplate. Extracted a single `iter_zig_imports(root) -> Iterator[tuple[Path, int, str, Path]]` generator and rewrote all five import-scanning functions against it тАФ each now reads as its predicate plus a one-line error append.

Also lifted `scan_compat_facade_imports`'s inline `{"model_transfer_types.zig", "model_runtime_types.zig", "model_surface_types.zig"}` set and `Path("core/abi/mod.zig")` literal out to module-level `_COMPAT_FACADE_ABI_EXEMPT_TYPES` / `_COMPAT_FACADE_ABI_EXEMPT_MODULE` constants. This removes the per-line set allocation inside the loop and names the exemption so a future reader can grep for it. Also fixed the missing blank line between `is_within` and the next top-level function (PEP 8).

`scan_lean_core` stays on the original pattern because it scans `.lean` not `.zig` and does not use the import regex.

Validation: `python3 -m py_compile runtime/zig/tools/check_core_import_fence.py` тЖТ PASS; direct run тЖТ exit 0, identical to pre-change (nothing in the tree currently violates the fence); `schema_gate` / `spec_diff_gate` / `pilot_evidence_gate` тЖТ PASS.

## Push: `webgpu_plan_executor_cli.zig` + `doe_queue_lifecycle.zig` DRY (2026-04-18 UTC)

Sixth random-file review fire, two Zig files, both functionality-preserving.

`runtime/zig/src/plan/webgpu_plan_executor_cli.zig`: `parseArgs` had five near-identical `if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, "--flag") and i + 1 < argv.len) { i += 1; out = try allocator.dupe(u8, argv[i]); continue; }` blocks. Lifted into a `tryConsumeStringArg(arg, argv, i, flag, allocator, out)` helper that returns `!bool`; five 5-line blocks collapse to five one-liner `if (try tryConsumeStringArg(...)) continue;` calls. Error behavior is preserved: a flag with missing value returns `false` from the helper, falls through to the next match attempt, and ultimately reaches the pre-existing `return error.InvalidCommandLine` at the bottom тАФ identical to the original short-circuit. The `--dry-run` boolean flag stays inline (no value to consume). CLI smoke with the full flag set still hits `error.FileNotFound` on the plan file (proving args parsed) and `--help` still returns `InvalidCommandLine` (preserving the "no help flag" contract).

`runtime/zig/src/doe_queue_lifecycle.zig`: `doeNativeQueueRelease` had three backend branches (Vulkan / D3D12 / else) each ending with the same 3-line common teardown (`const dev = q.dev; alloc.destroy(q); native_exports.doeNativeDeviceRelease(toOpaque(dev));`). Restructured as a single `switch (q.dev.backend)` over the backend-specific drain, followed by one copy of the common teardown. Also replaced the `if (cast(DoeQueue, raw)) |q| { ... }` outer indent with an early `orelse return`. Same release semantics on every backend; outer-nesting flattened by one level.

Validation: `zig build` тЖТ PASS; `zig build test` тЖТ PASS; `zig build test-wgsl` тЖТ PASS; CLI smoke (`--help`, full flag set) тЖТ expected errors preserved.

## Push: `adhoc_claim_gating.py` + `metal_pipeline_cache_manifest.py` DRY touches (2026-04-18 UTC)

Fifth random-file review fire. Two `bench/lib` files, both functionality-preserving.

`bench/lib/adhoc_claim_gating.py`: `gate_workload_claim` had three near-identical sample-count-floor blocks (baseline / comparison / warm-comparison), each 4-5 lines of the same `if count < floor: reasons.append(f"{label} sample count {count} < ...")` pattern. Lifted into a closure `_check_sample_floor(label, count)` that captures `reasons` and `policy`, then replaced the three blocks with three one-line helper calls. The warm-comparison branch's `is not None` check now lives inside the helper (as `count is None or count >= min_timed_samples`), so the call sites are uniform. Behavioral harness covers four cases тАФ all-green local, baseline-below-floor, warm-below-floor, p99-missing release тАФ and all match pre-change outputs.

`bench/lib/metal_pipeline_cache_manifest.py`: `commands_dispatched_kernel_names` checked `if kind not in ("kernel_dispatch",):` тАФ a single-element tuple that read as "future-proofing" but today just obscured a plain equality. Replaced with `kind != "kernel_dispatch"`, folded into the same isinstance check above it. Behavioral harness confirms the set of recognized dispatch entries is unchanged (accepts `kind` and `command_kind` aliases; picks up `kernel` and `kernel_name` aliases; strips `.wgsl` and directory prefixes).

## Push: `bench/gates/module_gate.py` dead-code + double-negative cleanup (2026-04-18 UTC)

Fourth random-file review fire. `bench/gates/module_gate.py` had three real issues:

1. **Duplicated import**: `from pathlib import Path` was imported twice тАФ once at line 7 before the `sys.path` manipulation, and again at line 20 with the rest of the imports. The second copy is a no-op; removed.

2. **Double-negative predicate**: the module-row aggregation computed `schemaOk` as `not any(not case_row["schemaOk"] for case_row in case_rows)`. That's `all(case_row["schemaOk"] for case_row in case_rows)` said the hard way. Replaced with the direct `all(...)` form to match the adjacent `correctnessOk` and `traceOk` lines which already used `all(...)`.

3. **Dead CLI flag**: `--json` / `args.emit_json` (`action="store_true", dest="emit_json"`) was declared in the argparse parser, then checked as `if args.emit_json or True:` тАФ the `or True` forced the JSON print to always run, making the flag a no-op. `grep` confirmed nothing in the repo invokes this gate with `--json`. Removed both the dead flag definition and the `or True` kludge; the gate now unconditionally prints the JSON payload (same observable output as before).

Validation: `python3 -m py_compile bench/gates/module_gate.py` тЖТ PASS; `--help` output matches the simplified surface; `schema_gate` / `spec_diff_gate` / `pilot_evidence_gate` тЖТ PASS (all three unaffected).

Third random-file review fire, one Python file and one Zig file from surfaces not yet touched.

`pipeline/agent/watchdog.py`: `build_candidate` declared a bare `dict` return type and had a stray leading space on its closing paren line. Tightened to `dict[str, Any]` per the bench Python style guide (modern built-in generics, not `typing.Dict`) and fixed the cosmetic indent. Added the `from typing import Any` import that the annotation needs. Round-tripped `python3 pipeline/agent/watchdog.py --input ... --output ...` against a two-toggle fixture тАФ identical JSON shape and ordering to pre-change.

Replaced with the parallel-slice iteration Zig has had for a while тАФ `for (parsed.value.toggles, entries) |t, *dest| { dest.* = ... }` тАФ which drops the index variable and writes through the pointer capture directly. Semantics are identical (slice lengths were already equal by construction). Same allocator-fallback-to-comptime-slice behavior on `dupe` failure is preserved.

Second random-file style review fire. `runtime/zig/src/full/surface_api.zig` had two tightenable spots:

Same semantics тАФ `CoverageEntry` is a plain struct of two `[]const u8` slice headers plus a `CoverageStatus` enum, so memcpy of the struct is identical to field-by-field assignment тАФ but expresses intent in one line per segment.
